Commentary

The Ministry of Finance Issues Emergency Decree 11

— Proclamation

To alleviate the current economic crisis in our country, the Ministry of Finance, referencing precedents from various nations, has issued an emergency decree. Effective today, banknotes issued by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications are designated as legal tender. All payments for grain taxes and all public and private debts must be settled using legal tender. The use of cash is prohibited, and violations will result in full confiscation to prevent the smuggling of silver. Furthermore, a Legal Tender Reserve Management Committee is established to manage the custody and issuance of legal tender reserves. This measure represents an unprecedented major reform in our country's currency system. The entire nation, whether in urban or rural areas, will be deeply affected by this reform. It is truly the most significant measure since the establishment of the National Government.

Our country has long been in a semi-colonial state, with the national economy suffering greatly from the oppression of imperialist powers. Not only has it been unable to develop, but it has also been declining daily. The global economic panic in recent years has forced major countries to abandon the gold standard one after another. As a result, the price of silver in the world has soared, and the value of our currency has risen accordingly, leading to deflation. Business bankruptcies have emerged repeatedly, capital is flowing out daily, and the balance of international payments is unfavorable. Although the government ordered the imposition of silver export tax and equalization tax on October 15th of last year, silver is still escaping due to the consistently high value of the currency. Now, the Ministry of Finance is resolutely implementing this long-considered monetary policy, aiming solely to prevent the complete outflow of silver reserves.

However, the critical issue of silver outflow lies in the decline of domestic industries and the dumping of foreign goods. While the government's current monetary policy can promote the development of national industries and achieve short-term effects, the fundamental solution lies in protecting domestic industries and preventing them from being further devastated by foreign forces.

Moreover, the direct impact of the government's policy implementation will be a sharp rise in prices. Low-wage workers in various industries may struggle to maintain their livelihoods. The government should be able to make appropriate arrangements regarding this matter of social stability. As for speculative merchants who seize the opportunity to compete for foreign exchange, as can be seen from the recent surge in the gold standard market, this is also expected. If so, the harm will be immeasurable. Fortunately, the Ministry of Finance has ordered the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications to buy and sell foreign exchange as much as possible to stabilize gold prices. The gold standard market can now avoid manipulation by speculators.

Four Near Eastern Nations Form Political Bloc Devoting Full Attention to the Far East, Allowing Britain and Russia to Have No Worries 12

(Tokyo) Turkey, Iran (Persia), and Iraq had previously entered into a non-aggression treaty and formed a political group. According to a telegram from somewhere on the 2nd, the Iranian Foreign Minister went to Afghanistan on the 31st to discuss with the Afghan government authorities and persuade them to join the group. This is clearly the behind-the-scenes work of Britain and Russia, who want to maintain the status quo in the Near East. Their ultimate goal is to allow Britain and Russia to have no worries in the Near East and prepare to devote full attention to the Far East. Therefore, the Japanese authorities attach great importance to this matter. (3rd, Dentsu)

Another Conspiracy by the Japanese Puppets to Destroy Soviet Railways Patrol Detachment Detains Criminals and Material Evidence 13

(Moscow) A message from Boli states that on the 26th of last month, six Koreans armed and intruded into Soviet territory. Northeast of Burtavka Station, they encountered a Soviet border patrol. The patrol immediately attempted to detain them, but the Korean bandits opened fire to resist arrest. As a result of the shootout, two Koreans were killed and two were injured. The remaining two disappeared during the conflict. Later, they encountered another Soviet patrol. The two opened fire on them. The patrol returned fire, seriously wounding one and allowing the other to escape. Subsequently, a large number of reactionary documents, two Browning pistols, two Mauser rifles, two pairs of pliers (used to remove iron rail spirals), and a grappling hook (to remove nails between rails and sleepers) were found at the scene. These items and the direction of the bandits' movements indicate that they intended to destroy the railway from Vladivostok to Grodekovo. This point was confirmed by the captured and injured bandits. They confessed that they were sent to Soviet territory by a certain military organization stationed at San Chako, and that after the first batch returned to Manchuria, the military organization would send a second batch of about seven or eight people to sneak into Soviet territory. (3rd, TASS)

At Dawn Yesterday, Italian Forces Launched General Offensive, Initiated Simultaneously on Northern and Southern Routes, Large-Scale Battle Plan, Abyssinian Forces Ordered to Defend Gorrahei Town to the Death 15

(Rome) The government has just issued a communiqué stating, "Our army began its offensive on all fronts at 6 a.m. The northern route is advancing towards Magale, while the southern route, the Somaliland troops, continue to operate in the Ogaden region. At the same time, the air force is also actively engaged in reconnaissance." (3rd, Havas)

(Rome) It is reported that the Italian forces on the northern route in Abyssinia have begun to attack Magale. This offensive is being undertaken jointly by the native soldiers commanded by General Biccheri Bellori and the troops of General Santini. The subordinates of the surrendered general Gugsa have joined the column commanded by General Santini and are accompanying the operation. Asmara If the Italian forces can occupy Magale, they will be able to advance and capture the highway connecting Tigray Province and Aksum, so Magale's position is crucial. This highway, which is 250 miles long, was built by the Abyssinian Emperor, and the Emperor may even be overthrown because of it. (20th, Guomin)

Vanguard of Italian Three Corps Advances 16

(Rome) According to a telegram from Asmara, the First Corps commanded by General Santini and the Ethiopian troops commanded by General Biroli are now advancing to attack Magale. Among them are a battalion of Blackshirts, Ascari soldiers, artillery, reserve troops, and 1,600 troops of Chief Kufsa, who surrendered to the Italian army. However, it was not mentioned whether the Second Corps of Aduwa would participate in this battle. Currently, a total of three corps have been ordered to launch a general offensive, with Magale as their main objective. Although the vanguard of the three corps advanced forward in the middle of this week, the main force is still very far from Magale. General Rudini's troops, who are attacking on the left flank from Adigrat, have reached the Meui Chi well, ten miles away. The Ethiopian troops attacking in the central road have advanced to the town of Hochien in the Ogaden region, which is very important from a political and military point of view. The Second Corps attacking on the right flank has sent an advance team from Aduwa along the commercial road to Magale, and it is now believed to have reached the Uli River. It is not yet known whether the main force on the right flank has returned. It is believed that General de Bono, commander-in-chief of the Italian forces in East Africa, is now planning a major offensive within days, with a line of defense starting from the Danakil Desert on the left, along the Chiwar River south of Magale, and then along the Takaze River to a point where the river forms the Eritrean border line. If this line of defense is occupied by the Italian forces, Magale will be included within it and will have penetrated deep into Abyssinian territory. It is estimated that it will take about two months to repair and consolidate it. It is now believed that General Graziani's large army on the southern route will advance from the desert of Walwal Dagega, with three detachments advancing along the Fanfan River from the Baihi Beri River Juba River to protect its left flank. The right flank is shielded by British Somaliland. General Graziani is likely aiming to encircle Gorrahei from two sides. The area is heavily fortified, and the defending forces have been ordered by the Abyssinian Emperor to defend the enemy to the death, so it will be difficult to take it. Also, it is reported that the Italian forces attacking from Assabai are still in the Musa Ali Mountain area and do not seem to have moved forward. (3rd, Reuters)

Hochien Town is a Key Military Location 17

Tigray Province Front Our correspondent with the army, Barr, reports that the first target of the Italian offensive is Hochien Town (60 kilometers southeast of Aduwa). General Santini's troops, who are in charge of the offensive, are advancing towards Hochien Town from the Maiwech outpost. There are also several columns of Italian troops and several teams of Ethiopian soldiers passing through the Donakil Desert, who will continue to advance after joining forces with General Santini's troops in Hochien Town. Hochien Town is a must-pass for camel caravans and is extremely important militarily. It is also the only route for advancing to the south. When the Italian forces attack, they must climb a plateau 2,000 meters above sea level. In addition to the aforementioned troops in charge of the offensive, the troops of General Maravigna stationed in Aduwa will also begin to move. At the same time, General Graziani, commander-in-chief of the southern route, will intensify the pressure on the Somaliland front. (3rd, Havas)

Using Natives as Guides 18

Tigray Province Front In addition to the original troops, the Italian army on the northern route now has a division of native soldiers, commanded by General Mariotti, which will also join the battle and attack the Abyssinian positions. This division is reorganized from the natives of the Donakil region. They have all joined the Italian army as individuals and have been incorporated into the Eritrean native ranks. The reason why they surrendered to the Italian army is that the Donakil region has recently been attacked by the main force of the Abyssinian army, which has caused them to join the Italian army in anger. When they met with the Italian military authorities, most of them held bows and arrows. The Italian army then made them change into military caps and uniforms and gave them rifles. Because the division is already accustomed to the harsh climate of the Donakil region, it is expected to be very helpful in covering the left flank of the Italian army in this operation. (3rd, Havas)

Tigray Province Front It is rumored that General Seyoum, the Governor of Grigri Province in Abyssinia, slandered General Gaza in front of the Abyssinian Emperor, and Prince Asa was also reportedly punished and demoted, and his post as commander of the garrison around Tessi was also removed. The Italian army has suffered heavy losses and has been forced to enter the Adal Desert, where the climate is harsh and long-term residence can be fatal. However, Italian aircraft still often scout in the Musa Ali area to search for the traces of the Abyssinian tribes. In addition, the correspondents of Italian newspapers stationed in the Abyssinian city of Jugra have said that the Italian army's attitude was very peaceful when it occupied the city. The Abyssinian government has protested against this statement, saying that the Italian army used bombs at the time and used terrorist tactics to deal with the civilians of the city. (2nd, Havas)

Marconi led his troops from western Abyssinia for seven weeks without stopping, and only arrived in Aksum yesterday. The Abyssinian Emperor's preparations for a motorcade and mule team to Tessi have been completed, and they are expected to depart on November 10. (3rd, Reuters)

Aksum According to a telegram from our special correspondent, Aochina, General Marconi, the governor of Ilubador Province in the easternmost part of Abyssinia, led his troops of 20,000 men to Aksum on foot, which took about a month to arrive. General Marconi once served as the Abyssinian ambassador to Italy and is an outstanding figure among the Abyssinian officials. All European expatriates in Abyssinia know him. This time, he led his troops to Aksum to defend the Emperor. His troops paraded through the streets in formation, and their discipline was very good. Most of the rifles they carried were "Grass-type" rifles purchased by the former Emperor Menelik 30 years ago. Although they are old, they are still very famous in the eyes of the Abyssinian natives because the victory of the Battle of Aduwa against the Italian army in 1896 was achieved with this type of rifle. In addition to a portion of the troops led by General Marconi carrying the aforementioned old rifles, the rest are equipped with new weapons and many machine guns. ((2nd, Havas)

Abyssinian Government Sends Note to the League of Nations Appealing for Financial Assistance Citing the 1930 Convention to Protect Peace and Resist Aggression 24

(Geneva) The Abyssinian government has sent a note to the League of Nations, requesting financial assistance to protect Abyssinia's peaceful existence and resist a country whose attitude endangers world peace. The note was published here tonight, stating that the League of Nations endorsed the draft convention on financial assistance in times of war or threat of war in 1930. When the Italian aggression occurred, Abyssinia had no army, let alone war materials. The Abyssinian government relied on the guarantee of collective security contained in the League of Nations Charter. It had neither established arms factories nor ammunition factories. The lifting of the ban on arms exports to Abyssinia by the League of Nations after Italy's aggression was of little help. Therefore, Abyssinia is appealing to the League of Nations for financial assistance to protect its peaceful existence. (3rd, Reuters)

(Geneva) According to the 11th League of Nations General Assembly on October 2, 1930, in accordance with Article 16 of the League of Nations Charter and the Finnish proposal passed in 1927, it was stipulated that financial assistance would be provided to the aggressed country. The signatories to this case included: Britain, France, Austria, Abyssinia, Spain, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, the Netherlands, Finland, Poland, and other 28 countries. The Abyssinian request this time is based on this case. (2nd, Havas)

Hoare-Laval Pact, Britain and France Cooperate to Seek Peace, League of Nations Authorizes Both Governments to Continue Reconciliation Efforts 27

(Geneva) The Sanctions Coordination Committee met at 4:15 p.m. First, French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval delivered a speech, saying, "France fulfills the League of Nations Charter with sincerity. France will comply with all programs jointly decided by the governments of all countries. On this day when we are taking important decisions, I would like to tell you that we still have another obligation indicated by the spirit of the League of Nations Charter, which must be fulfilled. In other words, we must find a way to resolve disputes in a friendly manner as soon as possible. Regarding this point, the British and French governments have agreed to cooperate. As far as France is concerned, it has a more urgent obligation than other countries because it signed a friendly agreement with Italy on January 7. Therefore, I will seek all the elements with unyielding perseverance to provide a basis for the negotiations. This is why I initiated diplomatic talks to resolve the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. However, I never want to make this talk have a definite nature outside the scope of the League of Nations because any suggestion or decision should be studied or adopted within the scope of the League of Nations. Today, people all over the world expect a lot from the League of Nations. I firmly believe that the League of Nations will fulfill its highest mission of peace and live up to the expectations of the public."

British Foreign Secretary Hoare then delivered a speech, saying, "We have no choice but to take collective action against Italy, which is regrettable. However, in order to be determined to maintain the principles of the League of Nations Charter and the collective security system, there is no other way but collective action. The purpose of our action is nothing more than to shorten the war. We also very much hope that it will succeed. However, in any case, we must continue to seek peace in an honorable way that can be accepted by all parties concerned. The speech recently delivered by French Prime Minister Laval fully represents the common view of all countries. I fully agree with it after listening to it. On the one hand, we are loyal member states of the League of Nations and have the strict duty to fulfill the obligations stipulated in the League of Nations Charter. On the other hand, we also have the same strict obligation, that is, to quickly obtain an honorable resolution of the dispute." Hoare then stated the situation of the recent diplomatic talks between Britain, France, and Italy, saying, "We all have the duty to review all possibilities for maintaining peace. We have done so in the past, and we will do so in the future. So far, the situation of the talks is only an exchange of preliminary opinions, and no specific results have been obtained. If these opinions can obtain specific results, then we will submit them to the League of Nations Executive Yuan for review as soon as possible in the most appropriate way. What we urgently desire is to establish a compromise under the auspices of the League of Nations. The Italian-Abyssinian dispute involves the League of Nations and the three parties of Italy and Abyssinia. We have not forgotten it. It would be a great injustice to say that we intend to establish an agreement that cannot be accepted by the three parties. I firmly believe that all of you present will approve of our actions, and you will also wish us success in our efforts to seek honorable peace."

Belgian Prime Minister Janson then delivered a speech, explaining the consistency of British and French actions, saying, "Since the governments of Britain and France are doing their best to find a solution, the League of Nations should entrust the two countries to carry out their work in the spirit of the League of Nations Charter and under the supervision of the Charter."

Soviet representative Potemkin said that the conflict in Africa is no different from the conflict in Europe. The only attitude that all countries can take is to resolutely implement sanctions. However, if a peaceful solution to the Italian-Abyssinian dispute can be established within the scope of the League of Nations, the Soviet Union will also welcome it.

Spanish representative Madariaga expressed his approval of the declarations made by Laval, Hoare, and Janson.

Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu expressed his hope in the name of the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente that peace would be restored under fair conditions in accordance with the spirit of the League of Nations Charter so that international obligations and the genuine friendship between these countries and Italy could be harmonized without conflicting with each other.

Then, Swiss representative Motta, Argentine representative Gnaschi, and Peruvian representative Totela successively delivered speeches, hoping that the Italian-Abyssinian dispute could be resolved peacefully in accordance with the Charter.

Finally, the Coordination Committee unanimously passed the proposal of Belgian Prime Minister Janson, entrusting the British and French governments to seek a peaceful solution. The meeting was adjourned by the Chairman of the Sanctions Committee, Vasconcelos, at 5:40 p.m. (2nd, Havas)

Britain, in the Mediterranean Sea, from east to west, from Alexandria, Egypt, to the Strait of Gibraltar, is like a chain, in which only the situation of Malta is clearly a weakness. The Military Situation Between Italy and Abyssinia 33

— Zhong Chi

——Geographical Observations

One

The Italo-Abyssinian War, which has shaken the world, has been raging for a full month since it broke out. The mechanized Italian army fought hard for three days and nights before finally capturing Adowa, a border town in Abyssinia. The humiliation of the Italian army's defeat in that town in 1896 was finally wiped away. Since then, apart from the continued fall of the sacred city of Aksum near Adowa, the Italian army has hardly achieved any significant victories. According to recent telegrams, the two armies on the northern front are engaged in fierce fighting in the area of Makale, north of the Tekezé River, and the two armies on the southern front are still in a stalemate near Walwal in the Ogaden region. Even if the Tigray Province and the Ogaden region all fall into Mussolini's hands, the Italian army will only have achieved preliminary victories. The more important and difficult decisive battles in the hinterland are yet to come.

Speaking of the war in the hinterland, the Italian army is not necessarily very confident. Originally, the Italian army only had significant advantages in weapons such as airplanes, tanks, and cannons. However, these modern weapons would lose most of their effectiveness in the high mountains of the Abyssinian hinterland. At the same time, judging from morale, especially from the terrain, the final victory may belong to the Abyssinian army. Now, let's examine the general trend of the Italo-Abyssinian War based solely on the geographical characteristics of Abyssinia.

Two

This time, Italy's large-scale invasion of Abyssinia began with its northern military base, Eritrea. This narrow strip of land along the Red Sea has a mild climate, suitable for Europeans to live in, and its central plateau is connected to the Abyssinian Plateau, making it a ready-made foothold for Italy to attack southward. However, Eritrea also has a major shortcoming, which is its sparse rainfall, which is almost always arid throughout the year. Therefore, this place has almost no products, but in terms of economic status, it is enough to control a small amount of the northern Abyssinia's overseas trade.

Italy obviously cannot obtain much economic benefit from this barren colony, so it covets the adjacent Abyssinian Plateau area. This is the only area in the entire Abyssinia suitable for colonization by Caucasians. Not only is the land relatively fertile, but the climate is also quite mild. The Amhara-speaking Abyssinians who believe in Christianity all live there, ruling the people of various races around them. We may use the entire area above 5,000 feet above sea level to represent this plateau area. Among them, there are many high mountains exceeding 10,000 feet, and the mountains in the north are even as high as 15,000 feet. At the eastern end of the plateau, the terrain suddenly drops, forming a large desert. This vast lowland, called the Danakil Depression, is the northern part of the Rift Valley. Some parts of the Danakil Depression are lower than sea level. This can be said to be the most desolate place in the world. Only two European expeditions have ever safely passed through this area. The leader of one expedition, Ludovico Nerbitt, gave it the name "trap of the underworld." The Rift Valley becomes narrower and narrower to the south, forming a ditch that separates the main Abyssinian Plateau from the Somali Plateau. Climbing the central plateau from the southern end of this Rift Valley is much easier than climbing from the northern area. The Gala people invaded Abyssinia from there in the 16th century.

The topographical feature of northern Abyssinia is the deep trenches formed by the Tekezé River and its tributaries that pass through the plateau. These river channels are often half a mile deep and have no bridges on them, which cuts off the invaders' advance from north to south. The Italian army in Eritrea has almost no way to penetrate into Abyssinia except by attacking southeastward through the Adowa area. Therefore, after the Italian army occupied Adowa, it attacked Magale and Mek'ele around the southeastern edge of the town's mountains. This route is the old route of the Italian army's invasion of Abyssinia in 1868.

The main target of the Italian army on this route is actually the mountains east and north of Lake Tana. The Atbara River, the Tekezé River, and the Blue Nile, on which the farmland of eastern Sudan and Egypt rely for irrigation, originate from these mountains. If the Italian army controls the sources of these rivers, especially the large reservoir of the Blue Nile, Lake Tana, then it will not only be easy to conquer Abyssinia, but it can also control the fate of Egypt and eastern Sudan.

However, it is very difficult for the Italian army to achieve such a goal. First, this offensive route passes through many high mountains and difficult-to-cross canyons, and there are almost no suitable roads and necessary bridges. The motorized Italian army cannot advance until the highway leading to Eritrea in the rear is built section by section and bridges are erected over the canyons along the way. Most of the materials used for bridge construction, road construction, and other military projects have to be transported from distant places. Even if the bridges, supply stations, and mountain roads hurriedly built by the road workers accompanying the army are completed, there is still a risk of being washed away by sudden flash floods at any time. Second, there are very few plains among the mountains of the Abyssinian Plateau. Except for the Lake Tana area and the basins of several other lakes, it is not easy to find a base for large armies to station. Such a terrain is only suitable for guerrilla warfare and not for modern tactics. Guerrilla warfare is what the Abyssinians are good at. In 1896, they relied on this tactic to win a glorious victory in Adowa. The deeper the Italian army penetrates into the plateau area, the more it has to be wary of being surrounded and attacked by Abyssinian guerrillas or having its communication lines cut off. Third, Abyssinia's agricultural products are only enough to supply the simple needs of the Abyssinian people. It is very difficult for the European expeditionary force to find the food and daily necessities it needs there. In fact, almost all of the Italian army's various military supplies have to be shipped from overseas to the plateau. Not only is the transportation cost extremely high, but this is also a difficult problem.

Three

Now, let's examine the military situation on the southern front. In this regard, the Italian Somaliland, the Italian army's base, is significantly different from Eritrea. This is part of the vast semi-desert region of East Africa. British and French Somaliland and northeastern and southeastern Abyssinia are all included in that semi-desert region. Italian Somaliland is close to the equator, and the climate is so hot that Caucasians often cannot bear it. The indigenous population is over one million, almost all living a primitive agricultural and nomadic life. The Juba River and the Webi Shabelle River originate from the northern plateau. If the Italian army wants to go to Abyssinia from the port of Mogadishu, it has to go up these two rivers, or pass through two hundred miles of barren desert before seeing the springs in Walwal, Gerlogubi, and other places. The military value of these springs is obvious.

The fierce fighting between the Italian and Abyssinian armies in the Ogaden region the other day was to争夺 these springs. However, Mussolini doesn't value the Ogaden region, which has few springs. He said that he didn't want to be a collector of "barren land." His preliminary military goals on the southern front are still several strategic locations in the northern part of the Somali Plateau in Hararghe Province. The Italian army is currently using Walwal and Gerlogubi as military bases to attack in that direction. If it occupies the strategic locations on the Somali Plateau, the Italian army will gain two major benefits: (1) The Italian army can control the entire basin of the two major rivers in Italian Somaliland, and (2) The Italian army can control the Hafasi River section of the Rift Valley; The Djibouti-Addis Ababa Railway passes through there. Even if this only way for Abyssinia to reach the sea is not occupied by the Italian army, the Italian army can still completely control it from the strategic locations in the northern part of the Somali Plateau.

However, there are also several difficulties in the advance of the Italian army on the southern front, namely, the hot weather, the long distance, and the lack of drinking water. Moreover, as on the northern front, while marching, it is necessary to build a motor road from the front line directly to the Indian Ocean, otherwise it will be inconvenient for supply. Even if it does not encounter fierce resistance from the Gala people and local Islamic tribes along the way, even if the Italian army occupies the lowlands and slightly higher areas of eastern or southeastern Abyssinia, the natural barriers of the plateau mountains are still not easy to break through.

Four

Although Mussolini intends to conquer the entire Abyssinia within this dry season, judging from the geographical situation of this invaded country, his wish may be difficult to fulfill. Moreover, the valiant resistance of the Abyssinian army over the past month is proving that the Abyssinian people are indeed a warlike nation. Although they lack modern weapons, they can resist foreign enemies with their natural barriers and brave spirit of defending their country. They have such difficult-to-attack terrain and can fully adapt to the local environment. In any case, this is an important military condition that the Italian army cannot match. The Abyssinian people can run 25 to 40 miles on rugged mountain roads every day without feeling tired for many days in a row. They raise local mules that do not need good feed, but are agile and hardworking, and can carry machine guns and small mountain artillery to any steep location. The Abyssinian army uses these weapons to create strong defensive lines that make the Italian army helpless.

If the Italian army cannot end the military operations in Abyssinia within the dry season, then the war will have to be suspended or delayed when the rainy season comes. Why? Because in Abyssinia, places below 6,000 feet above sea level are covered with a kind of yellow mud, which is dry and brittle in the dry season, but turns into soap-like mire when it rains, making it impossible to walk even on the road. If tank teams encounter a rainstorm in the yellow mud area, they will inevitably get stuck in the mire and have to wait until the sun dries the soil before they can move.

The Italo-Abyssinian War may evolve into a protracted guerrilla war after this dry season. Didn't Cyrenaica in Libya have about twenty years of guerrilla warfare? That place is much closer to Italy, and the number of Islamic residents is less than 200,000. If the Italian army's invasion of Abyssinia really lasts for a long time, then the Italian side's costly military expenditure and the sacrifices of the people may cause serious problems at home.

Page 7

Mayor of Beiping, Yuan Liang, Resigns with Approval; Song Zheyuan to Serve Concurrently on a Temporary Basis, to Assume Office on the 6th; All Departments and Sections of the Municipal Government are Prepared to Hasten the Handover 34

(Beiping) Mayor of Beiping, Yuan Liang, had repeatedly telegraphed the Central Government to earnestly resign due to long and arduous political service. He had been repeatedly persuaded to stay. Yesterday, he again telegraphed the Executive Yuan to reiterate his previous request with firm wording. He has now received a telegraphic reply approving his resignation. The original text reads: "To Mayor Yuan Wenqin, my esteemed brother, I have read your telegram and understand your request to resign as mayor. Your sincerity and earnestness are acknowledged, and approval is granted. Beiping is a strategically important location, and its affairs cannot be halted for even a day. The vacant position of mayor shall be temporarily concurrently served by Song Zheyuan. In addition to separate orders, you are expected to comply. Wang, President of the Executive Yuan, Seal of Kong on behalf of Jiang."

(Beiping) After Yuan Liang's resignation was approved, Zhu Zheyuan is scheduled to temporarily assume the position of mayor on the 6th. (Special Dispatch, 3rd)

(Beiping) After Mayor of Beiping, Yuan Liang, received the order of approval from the Executive Yuan today, he immediately ordered all departments and sections to prepare to expedite the handover. (Special Dispatch, 3rd)

Bandits Active Again on the Great Wall Line 36

Japanese Troops Stationed in Tianjin Repeatedly Cross Borders to Arrest People 63

Tianjin correspondent, residents here are living in fear because the Japanese garrison is arbitrarily arresting citizens across the border, causing extreme anxiety in society. The truth of the Chinese people arrested is described as follows:

At about 7 p.m. on October 28, vehicles Nos. 2-1993 and 2200, rented by the Japanese military, suddenly arrived at the Tianjin News Examination Office with 19 plainclothes Japanese military police. After entering the gate, they went straight to the office to inquire about the person in charge. At that time, Director Zhuang Yuling was out and had not returned. Deputy Director Wang Yifan received them and asked about their intentions. The Japanese said that the consulate had something to ask and asked him to go with them. Afterwards, they forced Wang Yifan and five staff members, Jiang Liangjun, Du Yunyu, Yao Jingxiu, and Zhu Yongnian, into the car and took them to the Japanese military headquarters in Haiguang Temple. At first, they were imprisoned in an ordinary room, and then they were taken to the detention center (detention center). Until the afternoon of the 29th, Du Yunyu questioned in Japanese about the reason for the arrest and asked for an interrogation. The staff officer Ishii questioned in detail about the organization of the news examination office, the meaning of the examination, and the root cause. Wang Yifan replied that the examination office was established under the central government's order to examine and suppress speech against the government and insipid remarks, and to censor reports and essays that would harm diplomatic relations according to the Good Neighborliness Order. Ishii said that such examinations were inevitably too passive. For example, the recent Xianghe incident was a genuine mass movement, so why not make efforts to publicize it? Wang replied that the examination office's authority can only check and withhold news, and cannot publicize any news. The right to publish similar incidents in Xianghe rests with the newspapers, and the examination office has no power to force them to publish it. Ishii was speechless and released them at 5 p.m. on the same day. Before they were released, the Tianjin Municipal Government had sent Secretary General Sun Runyu and Japanese Secretary Liu Shaoxian to visit the Japanese military headquarters and the Japanese consulate to inquire about the truth of the arrest, but they refused to tell the truth. It was not until the people were released that they knew the reason for the arrest.

Nian Guangyao, executive committee member of the Tianjin Chamber of Commerce, was arrested by the Japanese military police and the police of the Third Branch of the Tianjin Public Security Bureau on October 29 at the Baoyang Hotel, also accused of being related to the Blue Shirts Society. He has not been released yet. Nian once served as a backbone member of a certain society and had many grievances with people. This summer, someone informed the Japanese side that Nian was a member of an anti-Japanese society. The Japanese side once sent someone to the Chamber of Commerce to investigate and protested to the municipal government. Nian resigned and did not work at the Chamber of Commerce, but he was still unable to avoid disaster.

Li Ming, director of the Second Section of the Tianjin Social Affairs Bureau (the bureau's reorganization order has not been issued yet, according to the organizational charter, Li is the position of section chief), returned to his home in the British Concession from Hebei at about 5 p.m. on October 30. When he arrived near the Jingang Bridge, he was suddenly stopped head-on by a car. Three Japanese men jumped out of the car, all in plainclothes, and told Li that they were military police from the Japanese Military Police Headquarters and were going to the headquarters in Qingdao for questioning. Under duress, Li was forced into the car and taken to the military police headquarters in the Japanese Concession. Li's chauffeur went back to report that Li was missing. On the 31st, the municipal government received the report and sent Japanese Secretary Liu Shaokun to inquire with the Japanese side. According to the Japanese side, Li was a member of the Blue Shirts Society, and the military police had received a report, so they arrested him. Negotiations are still underway, and there is no news of his release. His family is also not allowed to visit. According to general investigations, Li has been the director of the Social Affairs Bureau for many years. In resolving previous labor unrest, he inevitably offended some people, so he was framed by traitors. (November 1)

Fuzhou: Commerce Increasingly Declining, Due to Stagnant Sales of Products 64

Fuzhou Newsletter: The commerce of Fujian Province is divided into two major regions: northern and eastern Fujian, with Fuzhou as the collection and distribution center, and southern and western Fujian, with Xiamen as the collection and distribution center. However, Fuzhou has always been an export port, while Xiamen has always been an import port. This is because tea, wood, paper, bamboo shoots, and other goods produced in eastern and northern Fujian are exported through Fuzhou. Most of these goods are sold to the Northeast and northern provinces. Since the fall of the Northeast, sales have dropped by more than half. Since the beginning of this summer, the Yellow River has caused disasters, and sales in the north have also been cut off. Export goods have plummeted, resulting in a change from export surplus to import surplus. As for imports, daily necessities from various counties in northern Fujian used to be transported from Fuzhou, and the amount of annual trade was huge. There was a so-called "Creek Transportation Gang" who specialized in transporting goods from Fuzhou to northern Fujian. Every year at the beginning of winter, merchants from northern Fujian came to the province to purchase New Year's goods, especially fine cloth, Suzhou and Guangdong goods, food, candles, and firecrackers. The market called this period the winter sales period. The annual profit and loss of the Creek Transportation Gang was determined during this period. However, this year, the winter sales period has already arrived, but the Fuzhou market is still very cold, and the business of the Creek Transportation Gang is even more declining. The reason for this is that half of it is due to the stagnation of sales of export products, the economic depression of society, and the weakening of purchasing power. The other half is due to the opening of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and the Fujian-Zhejiang Highway, allowing goods to be transported directly from Shanghai to various counties in northern Fujian via the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, and the Fujian-Zhejiang Highway (the Fujian-Zhejiang Highway connects from Jiangshan and passes through Pucheng, Jianyang, Jian'ou, and reaches Yanping), which is much simpler than transporting goods from Shanghai by sea to Fuzhou and then from Fuzhou by river to northern Fujian. Therefore, merchants abandon the former and choose the latter. There are still some merchants who come to the province to purchase goods because Shanghai requires cash payment, while Fuzhou can repay in installments. Therefore, merchants generally expect that after the completion of the Fujian-Jiangxi Railway, Yanping will become the commercial distribution center in northern Fujian, and the Fuzhou market will be naturally eliminated due to changes in the inland transportation situation. The provincial government is now requesting the central government to extend the Fujian-Jiangxi Railway from Yanping to Fuzhou to maintain the prosperity of the provincial capital, but it is not known whether it can be realized. In addition, Fuzhou has recently experienced a surge in bankruptcies due to poor business conditions, and the order of the market is very chaotic. The provincial government has specially ordered the Public Security Bureau and the County Chamber of Commerce to jointly form the Provincial Capital Store Bankruptcy Liquidation Committee, with Public Security Bureau Chief Li Jinde and Chamber of Commerce Chairman Luo Mianhou serving as the chairman and vice-chairman respectively. Stores that are unable to operate due to poor turnover can request the committee to find ways to maintain or mediate. Those who deliberately abscond will be strictly investigated to curb the bankruptcy trend. (November 2)

Songjiang: Summary of Winter Defense Meeting

In the Punan districts of this county, banditry has occurred frequently. As the winter defense season is approaching, the county government specially convened a winter defense meeting yesterday, attended by the Public Security Bureau, the 12th Security Brigade Headquarters, and the district chiefs of each district. County Chief Li presided over the meeting. Zhao Zanchen, the adjutant of the Security Brigade, presented cases regarding increasing defenses, joint defense, meeting sentries, and protecting vehicles, which were discussed in detail. Regarding the defense of the urban area, it was decided to follow the previous session's established case, which will be implemented from the 16th of this month.

Suzhou: Agricultural Bank of China Warrants Arrest of Absconding Staff Member

Wang Cainan (Zhengrong), the director of the cashier department of the Suzhou Agricultural Bank of China, absconded with 150,000 yuan of public funds, and there has been no news of his whereabouts so far. The bank has now offered a reward of 3,000 yuan for his arrest. After this incident occurred, Hou Houpei, the deputy governor of the head office, came to Suzhou in person to investigate. It was learned that another important staff member had embezzled more than 40,000 yuan, and there were also corrupt practices in the collateral section. Therefore, the head office ordered the governor of the Suzhou branch, Zhu Qingzeng, to return all the funds released in his hands within the year. It is also heard that there are plans to reorganize the Suzhou branch. The Suzhou branch has a total deposit of more than 800,000 yuan. Since the incident of Wang Cainan's absconding occurred, a large amount has been withdrawn. Fortunately, the branch has sufficient reserves and can still cope with it easily.

Reorganization of Business Corps into Civilian Defense Teams

Each branch of the Suzhou Business Corps was originally scheduled to start defense on the 15th of this month, assisting the police and maintaining local public security. The necessary defense funds have been requested from the County Chamber of Commerce. Recently, the County Government was instructed by the Provincial Government to abolish all business corps immediately and reorganize them into civilian defense teams under the command of the town chiefs and baojia chiefs. Therefore, the head of the corps, Ji Xiaosong, will convene a meeting of the heads of each department within days to discuss all the closing arrangements.

Changshu: Fire Brigade Conflict with Telephone Company

The conflict between the Central District Fire Brigade and the Telephone Company here is escalating. The Fire Brigade has stopped responding to fire alarms, and all the workers of the Telephone Company have gone on strike at the same time, with both sides standing in opposition. The reason for this incident is that the Central District Fire Brigade, in order to receive news quickly, connected a switchboard at the motor of the Zui Jing Ge Bookstore. The company considered this a violation of the regulations and confiscated the Fire Brigade's switchboard and cut the bookstore's telephone line, suspending the call. This caused negotiations. The Bureau Chief of Public Security mediated it, and reconnected the telephone of Zui Jing Ge first. Unexpectedly, the fire brigade reconnected the switchboard, and the Telephone Company sent craftsman Yang Shun Gao to remove it, but they were beaten by Wang Guo Liang and others from the fire brigade, which intensified the conflict. Because the Telephone Company workers were beaten for no reason, they announced a complete strike, believing they had no protection. The fire brigade has also made a major alliance, and formally announced cessation of fire fighting activities, further escalating the situation. The telephone company is planning to sue the county government.

Japanese Residents Come to Changshu for Sightseeing

On the evening of the 2nd, eight Japanese employees of the Datong Shipping Company on Sichuan Road, Shanghai, Hiroya Masashi, Nakayama Masahira, Yasawa Yoshitsugu, and Koazuma Masao, accompanied by a Chinese man Ye Qing, came to Changshu for sightseeing in their own cars. In the evening, when they were dining at Jin Fang Yuan, they summoned many prostitutes. The Public Security Bureau went to detain the prostitutes because calling prostitutes violated the prohibition regulations. As for Japanese businessmen traveling in the inland, many plainclothes police officers were specially sent to protect them and monitor their actions.

Provincial Committee Inspects Opium Suppression

The Provincial Opium Prohibition Committee, in order to examine the opium prohibition work of the branch committees in various counties and the business situation of opium paste shops, specially sent members to visit each county for assessment. Wu Xie, who was sent to this county, arrived on the 1st of this month. He first went to the fourth section of the county government to adjust the volume for inspection, and set off on the 2nd to visit the opium paste shops and smoking cessation hospitals.

Wuxi: Representatives Assembly of Rice and Bean Industries

This county's rice and bean industry, where merchants carry goods and sell them together, has a long-standing practice of mortgaging rice and grain stores to banks for funds, without issuing promissory notes. Indirectly, the banks are responsible for the loan. Recently, the banks in this county have intended to change the grain mortgage regulations, requiring promissory notes for warehouse receipt mortgages, otherwise it would be difficult to use. The bean industry believes that this encroaches on their business rights and sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce to consult with the Banking Association and ask them to postpone the implementation. Now, the Rice and Bean Industry specially convened a meeting of eight section representatives on the 3rd to discuss the banks' change of grain mortgage methods. It was decided that banks should be responsible for ordering merchants to issue promissory notes, but property rights should be protected. Otherwise, the merchants would be acting on behalf of their customers, and the responsibility would be difficult to establish, and there would be no way to grip the situation. Banks should be asked to issue receipts to prove it, which would be fair. For the customers, the old cases should be re-examined and all should sign pledges to provide security and responsibility. In addition, the association will designate Li Zhongchen to go to Shanghai to gather at the Fifth Plenary Session and petition to abolish the Guangdong special donation case for the miscellaneous grain and oil industries across the country.

Changzhou: Business Corps Abolished by Order

The Wu county business corps, organized by the County Chamber of Commerce, has managed by a separate commission and have done well in years of drills and rectifications. Recently, the County Government received an order from the province, to unify local military powers in order to actually carry out the security system, all business corps names in towns of the various counties are cancelled from November 1, and it should be reorganized into the civilian defense reserve team or watchtowers. The County Government immediately ordered the County Chamber of Commerce Headquarters and directed the various detachments and teams to act accordingly. Meeting with the district and town chiefs, baojia chiefs and other chiefs should immediately reorganize the watchtowers, and send a roster for reporting. Later the County Governor is responsible to send members to train in order to improve.

Zhenjiang: Dredging of Fragrant Herb River Not Extended

Danyang's dredging of the Xiangcao River was originally scheduled to begin on November 15 of this year and be completed on March 15 of next year. The Danyang Grain Food Industry telegraphed the Construction Department asking for a month's extension to allow Danyang's bulk agricultural product, brown rice, to be sold in time to avoid being shelved and missing the opportunity. After receiving the report, the Construction Department rejected the extension on the grounds that the river must be dredged during the slack season when the water is dry to avoid delaying the opportunity, and that the dredging period would not hinder the transportation and sales of grain.

Yangzhou: Transportation Bureau Acting as Agent for Honghu Dike

The Jiangbei Transportation Engineering Bureau believes that the Jiangbei Honghu Dike should be handled by the Guidong-Huaihe River into the Sea Engineering Office. The Guidong-Huaihe River into the Sea Engineering Office said that it was busy with engineering work, and sent a letter to the agency to be responsible for acting as an agent. Yesterday (the 1st) it ordered Feng Dan, the director of the Huaiqi section engineering office, to be responsible for handling the project. The required expenses of 80,000 yuan should be provided in three phases. In addition, the construction of the floodgates in the Xiangyun East-West Dyke project has been slowed down for the purposes of irrigation. Now it has also borrowed funds from the Agricultural Bank of China and notified Renchang Construction Factory, the contractor for the dike, to sign supplementary articles in order to complete it on schedule. The time limit is fifty clear days.

Huaiyin: Completion of Two Major Constructions

The county's urban and rural telephone network was installed in late October and was officially opened for calls and business on the 1st of this month. Generally, the fee is one cent per Chinese mile. In addition to District 1, the locations where calls can be made include five in Districts 2, 3, and three in District 4, and one in Matou Township. If you want to call outside this county, you can also connect with the provincial exchange. In addition, the Qingjiang Zheng and Yue floodgates outside the East Gate are the daily traffic arteries between urban and rural areas. The Four Floodgates Management Office had previously said that the two floodgates had been in disrepair for years, and all the paved boards on the floodgates and the beams under the floodgates were to be replaced. The Yue floodgate has been dismantled and repaired first, and the work has been completed long ago. Now the Zheng floodgate has been continuously repaired. After a total of one week, the work was completed on the evening of October 31. Traffic was officially restored on the morning of the 1st.

Hangzhou: Yu-Nan Section to Be Completed by the End of This Month

Along the line of the Yu-Nan section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, malaria was previously prevalent and spread very severely. Many road workers were infected and died, which affected the progress of the project. After sending personnel with a large number of drugs for prevention and treatment, the epidemic gradually subsided. The track laying project reached Geyang on the 1st of this month. From the 3rd, the construction train will sell passenger tickets, but because the location is remote, it will not be officially opened for business for the time being. The track-laying project for the entire section will be connected with each other by the 25th of this month, and the Thirteen-Arch Liangjiadu Bridge has completed ten of them. The Guixi Bridge is scheduled to be completed by the end of this month, and the entire section will be completed. The opening ceremony will be held in early December.

Ningbo: Cooperative Director of Fritillaria Bulb Arrested

Since the Fritillaria Bulb Transportation and Sales Cooperative was established in November 1932, disputes have arisen due to poor management. The Construction Department suspended the directors and supervisors of the cooperative and appointed Ding Xitang, Ni Weixiong, and Zhang Tong to take over and reorganize it. After the reorganization committee members went to the cooperative on the 30th to take over, they found in the handover of accounts that the directors of the cooperative had embezzled and engaged in corrupt practices. The directors of the cooperative, Zheng Jiahao, Cui Qianyu, Xu Youheng, Wang Yuankang, Yang Jinduan, Liu Qiyin, Cui Yongmao, and Xu Xilin, were all detained and escorted to the Yinxian District Administrative Inspector's Office for verification. That night, they all paid bail and were released to await interrogation.

U.S. Vice President Garner and Others Depart for the Philippines Yesterday Morning Aboard Original Ship; Issues Farewell Letter to China Before Leaving Shanghai 67

U.S. Vice President Garner, Speaker of the House of Representatives Byrns, and a congressional delegation totaling 134 men and women traveled from the United States to the Philippines to attend the inauguration ceremony of the new government. En route, they passed through China, arriving in Shanghai on the morning of the 2nd aboard the Dollar Steamship Lines' President Grant from Japan. They were warmly received by Chinese authorities and American officials and residents. With the inauguration ceremony of the new Philippine government approaching, they concluded their social engagements and, that evening, accompanied by a welcoming delegation from the Philippines, including Delgado, Coffila, Pacis, Onan Kakiao, Zamora, and Osman Nalla, departed in batches from the Customs Wharf around midnight aboard small ferries, returning to their original ship. They set sail from Shanghai at 4:30 AM yesterday, planning to attend the inauguration ceremony of the new Philippine government on the 15th of this month. Afterward, they will depart the Philippines on the 20th aboard the President Jackson, returning home via the same route through Shanghai.

The Central News Agency reports that U.S. Vice President Garner issued a farewell letter to China before departing Shanghai yesterday morning, which was submitted to the Central News Agency for publication. The translation is as follows: "I, on behalf of the government of the United States and the Congressional delegation to the Philippines, express our deepest gratitude to the Chinese people for their warm hospitality. Special thanks are due to Minister Kong and Mayor Wu for their kind invitations to grand banquets and tea parties. All this kindness has further strengthened our feeling of the sincerity and friendliness of the Chinese people, and our belief in the boundless growth of amity between the Chinese and American peoples. We regret that our visit was so brief, but we hope to have the opportunity for a more leisurely discussion when we return from the Philippines in the future." John Nance Garner (signed)

Dai Chuanxian and Ma Chaojun to Arrive in Shanghai Together Today; Will Take Ship South Tomorrow to Convey the Opinions of Various Committee Members; Chen, Li, and Others to Accompany Them North to Attend the Plenary Session 68

The Xin Xin News Agency reports that the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee officially opened on the 1st of this month. As a result, the number of attending committee members is unprecedented in this session, a cause of great joy not only to comrades within the party but also to the entire nation. Unexpectedly, Premier Wang was unfortunately injured in an assassination attempt by thugs shortly after the opening ceremony. Upon hearing this news, public sentiment was outraged. The Assembly, in addition to telegraphing a detailed report of the assassination of Premier Wang to all parties, decided to dispatch two members, Dai Chuanxian and Ma Chaojun, to travel south as quickly as possible to urge Central Committee members Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, and others, who are staying in Guangdong and Guangxi, to come north to Beijing as soon as possible to attend the session. This would fully demonstrate the spirit of unity and struggle. According to inquiries by the Xin Xin News Agency, Dai and Ma are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai from Beijing on the 4th and will board the Empress of Asia, which departs from Shanghai on the 5th, to travel south and meet with Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, and others, conveying the opinions of the committee members in Beijing. Sources also indicate that the reason Chen, Li, and others have been unable to come north to attend the plenary session is that they are tied down by military and political affairs and cannot find the time to leave Guangdong. Now that the Central Government has repeatedly urged them, they will certainly make time within the realm of possibility to travel to Beijing to attend the plenary session and jointly deliberate on national affairs. After meeting with Dai and Ma, they may travel north together by plane.

The Money Trade Association Held an Emergency Meeting Last Night 71

Rumors have been rampant in recent days, leading to large-scale manipulation by speculators. The prices of all goods have soared, and even subsidiary coins, such as fractional silver dollars and copper coins, have experienced significant price increases. In particular, the money shops, facing pressure from depositors and a shortage of reserves, have found it difficult to cope. Last night, the difference between official reserves and actual reserves reached over 17 million, making it impossible to cover. The Money Trade Association immediately convened an emergency meeting of the executive committee last night to discuss remedial measures. Until 12:00 midnight, the result was to deposit all the cash of the money shops with the Central Bank, and request that the bank issue banknotes to help relieve the market.

Australian Mission to Shanghai Commercial Commissioner Hopes That Domestic Industrial and Commercial Leaders Will Quickly and Carefully Review Past Losses of Our Country 73

The Huadong News Agency reports that Mr. Wang Gongfang, Vice-Consul of our country's Consulate General in Sydney, recently sent a letter to the International Trade Bureau, detailing the mission of the newly appointed Australian Commercial Commissioner to Shanghai and the future of Sino-Australian trade. The following is a record of the investigation by the Huadong News Agency reporter: (Omitted above) Among the Eastern countries, Australia's trade is most important with China, Japan, and the Dutch East Indies. In recent years, the export of Australian agricultural products, meat, butter, etc., to England has been captured by South American countries such as Argentina, which has had a significant impact. Therefore, it is urgent to change the policy and find new markets in the East to compensate. In April of last year, after Australian Foreign Minister Latham visited various countries in the East, he proposed sending commercial commissioners to China, Japan, and Nanyang. Due to careful selection of personnel, the time was slightly delayed. In May of this year, the official appointments of the principal and deputy commercial commissioners to the three places were successively announced. The appointed Commercial Commissioner to Shanghai is Mr. Bowden, V.G. Bowden, and the Deputy Commercial Commissioner to Shanghai is Mr. Nutt, A.L. Nutt. Mr. Bowden returned to Australia in May of this year to travel to major ports with Mr. Nutt to contact and discuss plans to promote Sino-Australian trade with local industrial and commercial leaders. Mr. Bowden and Mr. Nutt arrived in Shanghai on September 9 to take up their new posts. Representatives stationed abroad by Australia include the Chief Representative appointed by the Commonwealth of Australia in London, England. The current incumbent is Bruce, who served as the Australian Prime Minister after the European War. He is permanently stationed in London to discuss various matters related to the entire Australia with the British government. The representative also serves as Australia's plenipotentiary representative to the League of Nations. In addition, the six states of Australia each send a representative to London. The six representatives are responsible for finding ways to promote the products of their respective states in England. Australia has a commercial office in Paris, which is controlled by the chief representative stationed in London. Since 1918, Australia has had a representative office in New York. In April 1929, a commercial commissioner was appointed in Toronto, Canada. In 1934, another commercial commissioner was appointed in New Zealand. In our country, a commercial commissioner was appointed in the tenth year of the Republic, with a general office in Shanghai and branch offices in Hong Kong. However, it was canceled in the twelfth year of the Republic because it did not achieve any results. When it was discussed again this time, there was considerable debate about the location in China. Some people advocated changing the location to Hong Kong, the reasons being (1) most of the overseas Chinese in Australia are from Guangdong, (2) the center of China's trade with Australia is also in Hong Kong and Guangzhou. However, others argued that Hong Kong belongs to British territory, and if stationed there, it would inevitably give the Chinese people an unpleasant feeling. In reality, Shanghai is indeed the commercial and financial center of China, and Guangzhou is second. The Australian government decided to adopt the latter proposal and stationed the Commercial Commissioner to China in Shanghai. In addition to the above-mentioned location decision, the selection of the Commercial Commissioner and his mission were also carefully discussed. The Australian government, learning from past mistakes, is determined to avoid past failures this time. Only by studying the reasons for past failures can we come up with a plan to correct them. Therefore, the Commonwealth Government's Ministry of Commerce and the Australian Committee on Trade with the East jointly formed a committee to select overseas commercial commissioners. Among the members of the committee was Dr. Melbourne, who had traveled to China and had a good understanding of the situation in our country and was known as a China expert. He wrote an article detailing the qualifications and tasks of the Commercial Commissioner to China, which were adopted by the Australian government. Reading its contents shows the policy and purpose of Australia's trade with China, and it is indeed opening a new situation in Sino-Australian trade. We should first understand the mission of their Commercial Commissioner, which is to increase the sales of Australian goods in China. However, judging from China's trade with Australia over the years, it has always been in an unfavorable position. There are many reasons for this. Now that they are sending personnel to China, they must know our country's needs, which are also stipulated in their duties. Can we afford to miss this opportunity? Therefore, it is hoped that domestic authorities and industrial and commercial leaders should quickly and carefully review the past losses of our country and the methods of remedying them in the future. This kind of unfavorable trade imbalance should be coordinated with our consulates in Australia to achieve effective cooperation. It is advisable to consult with the Commercial Commissioner on effective improvement measures.

Central Trust Bureau Responds by Telegram, Resolving Not to Let Sino-French Savings Account Holders Suffer Losses; Will Announce the Reorganization Plan as Soon as It is Completed 74

The Sino-French Savings Society, by order of the Ministry of Finance, stopped accepting deposits on July 4, and was taken over by the Central Trust Bureau and the branches of the Central Bank in various places. After completion, the Central Savings Society will open for business. The Shanghai General Bureau has replied by telegram, "As soon as the reorganization plan is completed, it will be announced. It is resolved that the interests of depositors will not suffer any losses."

Allocating Funds to Promote Acceptance Bills; The Banking and Money Industries Held Separate Meetings; To Be Submitted to the Ministry for Approval and Implementation After a Decision Is Made; The Purpose Is to Adjust Finance and Increase Chips 76

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee accepted the suggestion of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and allocated 3 million yuan to promote the acceptance bill fund method. After passing, it sent official letters to solicit consent from the banking and money industries. It is scheduled to be discussed and the details are as follows:

The Banking and Money Industries Discussed Separately: The Committee, considering the industrial and commercial credit small loans, has been in operation for three months, and the amount released is only 200,000 yuan. Now, to support industry and commerce, it has been decided to allocate 3 million yuan from the loan items recognized by the banks and money industry as a fund for promoting industrial and commercial acceptance bills and discounting. The treasury vouchers issued by the Ministry of Finance are the second guarantee. After the method was passed, official letters were sent to the Banking and Money Industry Associations and the Central Bank to solicit consent. Now, the Money Industry Association has decided to submit it to the Executive Committee meeting on the 10th for discussion, and the Banking Industry Association will also submit it to the Executive Committee meeting for discussion. The Central Bank has submitted it to the Business Bureau for review.

To Be Implemented After Approval: The Xin Sheng News Agency reporter learned from the banking and money industries yesterday that the Banking and Money Industry Associations and the Central Bank are expected to agree to the industrial and commercial loan review committee's approved method of promoting acceptance bills. After replying to the committee, it will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation. They all believe it is very appropriate. In the future, it will be handled by the lending banks and money houses, but it must be submitted to the relevant committee for review and approval of treasury bills. The purpose is to adjust finance and increase chips.

The Second Special District Citizens' Association Again Writes to the Municipal Council; Opposes Telephone Charges Based on Usage; If the Company Is Determined to Implement Usage-Based Charges, All Users Will Have No Choice but to Refuse to Pay 81

Regarding the telephone company's attempt to implement usage-based charges, all users are opposed. The Second Special District Citizens' Association of the French Concession, based on the opinions of all citizens in the district, previously wrote to the French Municipal Council to forward the letter to the telephone company to stop the plan. The association again wrote to the Municipal Council yesterday, asking it to forward the letter to the company and urging it not to implement the plan. The original letter states: "To the French Municipal Council: After the Shanghai Telephone Company requested to increase user rental fees and adopted a usage-based charging method, our association has written to your council to ask it to find a way to stop the plan. We have learned that the Telephone Expert Committee has completed its review, and its report acknowledges that the telephone company should obtain a net profit of 10% by fulfilling the franchise contract. As for its charging method, commercial telephones are charged 10 yuan for 150 calls per month, and household telephones are charged 6.5 yuan for 100 calls per month. An additional charge of 3 fen is levied for each extra call. If calculated according to these numbers, commercial telephones are limited to only 150 calls per month, averaging only 5 calls per day, and household telephones are limited to only 100 calls per month, averaging less than 4 calls per day. However, commercial and household use is much more than 5 or 4 times a day. How much will the price increase if it doubles? How much will the price increase if it triples? The commercial depression is now extremely serious, so how could they bear this heavy burden? Furthermore, if the company restricts calls so strictly, if commercial and household users remove telephones due to low efficiency, or only keep one of the two, or use two-fen postage to communicate, or if they take other measures because they cannot afford to make more than 5 or 4 calls a day, how will the company obtain a 10% net profit? The Expert Committee has not considered this, and only focuses on maintaining the company's net profit. The company is only concerned with its own generous annual interest, without considering whether users can afford it. It insists on going its own way and will not relent. Our association, representing all citizens, cannot agree to this plan. If the company must implement usage-based charges, all users will have no choice but to refuse to pay and let the company remove the telephones. As it relates to social welfare, we are writing to your council again to ask it to consider the public opinion of the citizens, and forward this letter to the company, so that the usage-based charging method will not be implemented in order to appease society and follow public opinion. We extend our best wishes to you and hope for your assistance."

Sincerely, The Second Session of the Directors and Supervisors of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Union, Jiang; (3) To the Secretariat of the Sixth Plenary Session of the Central Party Headquarters in Nanjing, for translation and forwarding to Premier Wang Jingwei: We were shocked and deeply alarmed to hear of the danger Your Excellency encountered. We hope that you will take care of yourself for the sake of the country and send this telegram to express our comfort and respectfully request your attention. Sincerely, The Second Session of the Directors and Supervisors of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Union, Jiang.

China Children's Welfare Association: Improving Infant Care Plans - Starting with Training Talent and Improving Equipment, Beginning in Shanghai and Then Expanding to the Whole Country 88

Guomin News reports that the China Children's Welfare Association, recognizing that infant care facilities in China are rudimentary and have many shortcomings in equipment, feeding, and hygiene, which greatly affect the life and health of infants, has specially hired child health experts Li Tingan, Zhang Ji, Yan Fuqing, Liu Yide, and others to draft a plan to improve infant care facilities, so that infant care facilities across the country meet modern and scientific standards. The plan will first be implemented in Shanghai and then expanded to the whole country. The details of the plan are as follows:

Training Talent: The China Children's Welfare Association believes that in order to improve infant care facilities, it is necessary to start with training talent. Therefore, the following guidelines have been set for talent: (1) The directors and existing staff will not be changed, but the directors will be actively requested to implement scientific equipment improvements; (2) Pediatric experts and doctors will be invited to voluntarily take charge of health matters in the facilities and conduct weekly check-ups; (3) Pediatric nurses with nursing diplomas will be hired to manage the cleanliness of the facilities, infant feeding, treatment of minor illnesses, and training of infant caregivers and wet nurses; (4) Ten infant care specialists will be recruited, with a junior high school education and aged 18 to 25. After graduation, they will stay in the facilities to work, specializing in infant nutrition; (5) Wet nurses must undergo physical examinations to check for diseases such as syphilis, gonorrhea, trachoma, and lung disease, as well as to check the quality of their breast milk. After being hired, they should learn basic infant care knowledge. The training of infant care specialists will cover the following subjects: A. Infant care methods such as bathing, bed making, dressing, feeding, etc.; B. Medical common sense; C. Bacteriology; D. Personal hygiene; E. Environmental hygiene; F. Infant nutrition; G. Isolation and disinfection methods; H. Education and visits.

Improving Equipment: Regarding the improvement of infant care facility equipment, it is proposed that the existing infant care facility buildings be used as usual, but the equipment must be improved according to scientific methods, adding infant care and medical departments, infant nutrition departments, infant outdoor recreation halls, bathhouses, sickrooms, isolation rooms, and sterilizers. Every infant care facility should have the following equipment: (1) Adding an infant care training class with ten students, graduating in two months, with food costs of 140 yuan and book costs of 30 yuan; (2) Adding a health and medical department, with equipment costs of 150 yuan; (3) Adding sickrooms, isolation rooms, bathhouses, hot water equipment, hot diaper pots, and disinfection equipment, totaling 300 yuan; (5) Adding an outdoor recreation hall, with equipment costs of 180 yuan, for a total cost of 1,000 yuan.
