Zhejiang Province Scenic Spot Guiding Bureau: Business Progresses Generally, Dividing the Province into Scenic Areas and Establishing Scenic Spot Management Offices 93

After the Southeast Transportation Exhibition concluded last year, the Zhejiang Province Scenic Spot Guiding Bureau followed, but due to the province's financial constraints, there was no fixed funding. Fortunately, Director-General Ye Jiajun made every effort and worked hard, and significant results have been achieved in the past year. Authorities in various provinces have recognized this and are competing to explore organizational methods to learn from it. Developing the guiding industry and attracting Chinese and foreign tourism investment is the only way to develop industry and commerce and subsidize the rural economy. The recent news of the bureau's work is recorded below for readers: (1) Dividing the province into scenic areas: The scenery in Zhejiang Province is natural and picturesque everywhere, and it has always been known as the "Switzerland of the East." Since the bureau's reorganization, it has become even more beautiful, and the number of tourists has increased sharply. For the convenience of management, the bureau has divided the province's scenic spots into seventeen scenic areas, namely West Lake, Linglong Mountain, Tianmu Mountain, Yandang Mountain, Tiantai Mountain, Qili Creek, Xuedou Mountain, Tiantong, Yuwang, Wuxie, Beishan, Xiandu, Fangyan, Nanming Mountain, Shimen Cave, Mogan Mountain, Putuo Mountain, and Yu Mausoleum; (2) Establishing Scenic Spot Management Offices: According to the above-mentioned scenic areas, a Scenic Spot Management Office is established in each area, all directly under the jurisdiction of the bureau to unify authority. Those that have been established include Tianmu Mountain and Qili Creek. The Xuedou Mountain management plan is under consideration. After being submitted to Chairman Chiang for approval, it can be established next spring. Other areas are also being planned and prepared; (3) Training qualified tour guides: China has no tour guides. Only Shanghai and Beiping have so-called "open-air guides" who are not adequately educated and have many bad habits, which greatly affect the international impression. The bureau created a tour guide training institute. The students' level is all above high school, and the training time is six months, with the first three months being classroom courses and the last three months being practical exercises. After the internship period is completed and qualified, official licenses are issued. The classroom courses have already been completed, and the qualified personnel have been assigned to various scenic areas for internships. Next spring, tourists visiting Zhejiang will have good guides; (4) Compiling Chinese and English guidebooks: Attracting Chinese and foreign tourists depends on effective publicity. Compiling and printing tourist guidebooks is an important task. Those that have been published include the scenic spots along the Hangzhou-Huizhou Road (including Linglong Mountain, Tianmu Mountain, Yuling Pass, etc.), Tiantai Mountain, Yandang Mountain, and the four scenic spots in eastern Zhejiang (Wuxie, Beishan, Xiandu, and Fangyan). There are eight types of tourist guidebooks in Chinese and English, and those currently being printed include West Lake, Qili Creek, and Xuedou Mountain. Other guidebooks are being written. These guidebooks all use three-color covers, with pictures and text, and the printing is very exquisite. The cost is high, and the expenses are large. Because there are too many requests and the postage is also expensive, a limited method has been set: each letter must be accompanied by five cents in postage; (5) Publishing transportation tour maps: The former Southeast Transportation Exhibition originally planned to publish this map, but it was not possible due to the short time. The bureau was originally responsible for handling the matters of the Southeast Transportation Exhibition, and it can be held next spring. This map is very important. The name of the map is "Southeast Transportation Tour Route Map," which has been published. All travel issues are covered. It is said that the China Travel Service, the two railway business offices, and the North Station information office in this city all sell it for two jiao each; (6) Adding an information office at Broken Bridge: The bureau's business is developing rapidly. Every day, there are dozens of inquiries by letter or in person. The bureau's address is in the Construction Department, which is inconvenient for tourists to contact. Therefore, the original site of the railway exhibition hall in front of Broken Bridge in West Lake has been renovated and transformed into a new information office, which is open day and night. A display window for local products of the province has also been set up to promote the trade of local products. The Shanghai Rotary Club travel group and the Guangdong team of the National Games sightseeing group were all planned by the bureau, and staff were sent to guide them. Everyone expressed satisfaction.

Yuantong Fish Company Announces Closure and Liquidation; Managers of Bankrupt Fish Companies Can Become Brokers at the Fish Market 94

The Guowen News reports that the business of Shanghai's fresh and salted fish companies has been poor in recent years, and the recent sluggish market has had a greater impact. Although this year's fish production is relatively small, the price has not risen as a result, and the fishing industry's economy is becoming increasingly panicked. The Yuantong Fish Company at 16th Pier in this city announced its closure and liquidation in this panic. The company's manager, Zhang Zhisheng, is a standing committee member of the Shanghai Salted Fish Association and has considerable experience in the fish industry, but he could not avoid closure and liquidation. Others can be imagined. According to people familiar with the fish industry, the fishing industry in this city has now entered a period of decline. During this period, the only way out for managers or employees of closed fish companies is to join the Ministry of Industry's fish market. Managers of bankrupt fish companies only need a deposit of 2,000 yuan to become brokers at the fish market, while operating a fish company alone requires no less than 20,000 to 30,000 yuan. Even for employees, the fish market is a government agency, and the salaries paid may not be lower than those of fish companies, so the living conditions can be relatively better. In the market, having people with fish industry experience to manage all affairs is also more convenient.

Beauty Hospital Shi Shuanghu Publicly Insults and Is Sentenced; Publicly Insulting Song Hongfu in the Newspaper; Trial Results in a Fine of Thirty Yuan 96

Shi Shuanghu, who runs a beauty hospital, saw that his student, Song Hongfu from Fenghua, had independently established the Shanghai Beauty Hospital after graduating from medical school, which affected his business. He asked Song to return the graduation certificate he had given him, but Song refused. Shi then published a statement in the newspaper, saying that Song had been practicing medicine for less than half a year and had started his own business, treating human life like grass. Song immediately filed a criminal self-accusation against Shi for obstructing his reputation. Dai Rongduo, a judge of the First Special District Local Court, held a hearing and summoned Shi for questioning, but Shi evaded and did not appear. After reviewing the evidence submitted by the plaintiff, Judge Dai found that the defendant Shi Shuanghu had indeed publicly insulted the plaintiff and sentenced him to a fine of thirty yuan, which could be commuted to one day of labor for each yuan of the fine. The reasons for the judgment were roughly as follows: The plaintiff submitted a Shenbao newspaper from September 12 of this year, with an advertisement published by the defendant titled "Important Statement by Dr. Shi Shuanghu, Director of the Modern Science Beauty Hospital, Canceling the Graduation Certificate of Song Hongfu, Director of the Shanghai Beauty Hospital." The words in the advertisement had the intent of insulting the plaintiff, such as "Medical aspects are full of errors," and "Now Song Hongfu has been practicing medicine for less than half a year and has started his own business, treating human life like grass," and "Fortunately, I hope that all sectors will be aware and not be harmed by this quack doctor." The meaning is very clear. The plaintiff was indeed a student of the defendant, but the defendant gave him a graduation certificate, indicating that his medical skills had reached a considerable level. How could he insult the plaintiff with words such as "quack doctor," "full of errors," and "treating human life like grass" after the plaintiff started his own business and publish it in the newspaper, making it public to everyone? He should undoubtedly be held responsible for the crime of public insult. The defendant was legally summoned but did not appear in court, so the judgment was made without waiting for his statement.

Five Years Later, the Yong'an Yarn Factory Bribery Case Opens; Tan Huanxiang, a Person Involved in the Case, Surrenders in Shanghai; The Court Summons All Parties for Interrogation and Schedules a Judgment 97

In 1930, the Yong'an Yarn Factory in Wusong experienced a labor strike. The company, through Tan Huanxiang and Hong Dongyi, bribed Yan Gunian, Jin Fan, Wang Yunchang, and other members of the labor union executive committee to resign, causing the union to stop working and easing the labor strike. Later, Yan and others reported the bribery situation. As a result, they were not prosecuted because they were not civil servants. Subsequently, the High Court ordered a re-investigation, but Tan and Hong were on the run, and the case was suspended for five years. Now, the old matter is being brought up again. Tan Huanxiang has now returned to Shanghai and works as a senior employee at the Xiang Sheng Automobile Company in this city. Fearing that he would be discovered by the court, he filed a self-surrender with the local court and was ordered to pay a 500 yuan bail. Later, the bail was increased to 2,500 yuan. At 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, Judge Jun Qinzhi specially opened the Fifth Court for interrogation. First, Guo Shun, the general manager of the Yong'an Yarn Factory, arrived in court and testified. He was 51 years old, from Guangdong, and lived at 1400 Jing'an Temple Road. The judge said, "Your case has already been concluded. Today, you are being summoned to court to testify. You should tell the truth." Guo said, "Yes, yes." The judge asked, "How many years have you been managing the factory?" Guo replied, "More than ten years." The judge asked, "How many factories are there in total?" Guo replied, "Four factories. The second factory was established in 1921, formerly known as the Da Zhonghua Factory. Because of business failure, we took it over." The judge asked, "When was the union established?" Guo replied, "I don't know." The judge asked, "After the union was established, what did it do? Did the workers automatically confront the factory?" Guo replied, "Their union had no relationship with our factory." The judge asked, "Were Yan Gunian and Jin Fan union leaders?" Guo replied, "I don't know. I don't know Jin Fan, but Yan Gunian was a bookkeeper in the Wusong factory." The judge asked, "Do you have any ill feelings towards Yan Gunian?" Guo replied, "No." The judge asked, "Did your factory pay any money?" Guo replied, "No." The judge said, "You have already been declared innocent, and the judgment is final. You can tell the truth." Guo replied, "There really was no such thing." The judge said, "Then why did Yan Gunian say that you took out 3,000 yuan to dissolve the union?" Guo replied, "No." The judge asked, "After the Party dissolved the union, did the union re-establish itself?" Guo replied, "I don't know." At this point, Guo's lawyer stood up and said that Guo Shun's daily duties were extremely busy, and he requested permission to leave first. The judge approved it and ordered Guo Shun to sign and leave. Next, Tan Huanxiang testified that Hong Dongyi borrowed 3,000 yuan from him, saying that it was borrowed on behalf of a friend to open a sock factory. He borrowed it from Yan Gunian, Jin Fan, Wang Yunchang, and others because he had no money. The judge asked, "What is your relationship with Yan and others?" Tan replied, "Union relationship." The judge said, "That's not right. You previously testified that Hong Dongyi wanted to borrow money, and you borrowed it from relatives, stating that it would be returned by January 4. At the end of December, you asked Hong for it without success, so you borrowed it from Yan Gunian, etc." Tan replied, "Yes, it's like that. I later returned it in two installments, first 2,000 yuan and then 1,000 yuan." The judge asked, "Was Chen Hanjian the secretary of the union?" Tan replied, "Yes." The judge asked, "On December 7, 1929, did you order Chen Hanjian to persuade Yan Gunian to resign?" Tan replied, "No such thing." The judge asked, "Chen Hanjian's business was recommended by you. He certainly has no ill feelings towards you. Why would he say that about you?" Tan replied, "I don't know." At this point, Chen Hanjian's agent, lawyer Shen Yong, stood up and said that Chen Hanjian was working in Qingdao, so he did not arrive. The judge then invited Prosecutor Xie Lian to the court, gave a lecture, and finally the defendant's lawyer stood up and requested that the defendant be found innocent. The judge considered the end and scheduled the judgment to be pronounced at 2:00 PM on the 9th of this month. Tan Huanxiang was still released on his original bail.

Silver Dollar Exchange Rate Drops Again 98

In the local silver dollar exchange rate market, two weeks ago, each silver dollar could be exchanged for 3,420 copper coins, and silver coins could be exchanged for about 12.40 yuan. In the past two weeks, the copper coins have hovered around 3,345 yuan, and the silver coins have fluctuated between 12.20 and 12.30 yuan. Until the day before yesterday (Saturday), each silver dollar could still be exchanged for 3,300 copper coins, and silver coins could be exchanged for 12.20 yuan. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, it suddenly fell sharply. Each silver dollar fell to 3,000 copper coins, and silver coins were only exchanged for 12.70 or 12.80 yuan. Therefore, the market was in great chaos for a while. The shops and stores arguing about the price of silver were heard everywhere.

Tea Shop Manager Secretly Sells Shop Base; Trial Begins; Proprietress, Still in Thin Clothing, Breaks Down in Tears; Manager Claims Justification for Closing the Shop—Court Postpones for Investigation and Further Examination of Witnesses— 99

Gong Bogao of Zhenjiang opened the Tianluchunji Tea and Food Shop at 449 Rue du Père Robert in the French Concession, operating it for six years until his death on August 24th of last year. His wife, Gong Sun, continued the business, entrusting its management to Sun Maokun, an old shop assistant and fellow townsman. Mrs. Sun returned to her hometown on August 17th of this year to commemorate the anniversary of her late husband's death. Unexpectedly, the very next day, Sun Maokun, through a lawyer, published a statement accusing the proprietress of absconding with funds, declaring the shop liquidated, and offering it for sale. In early September, Mrs. Sun returned to Shanghai from her hometown and learned that the manager had secretly sold the shop, allegedly embezzling the proceeds and outstanding debts. She then engaged lawyers Fan Gang and Ma Lemon to file a suit in the Second Special Court's Criminal Division, accusing Sun Maokun of breach of trust and embezzlement. The court accepted the case and initially summoned the defendant, but he failed to appear, so a new hearing date was set. Previous reports have covered these details. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Li Changnian of the Second Special Court continued the trial in the Second Criminal Court. Plaintiff Gong Sun, accompanied by her lawyers, appeared and reiterated her previous statements, requesting the return of the shop base and the embezzled funds. She stated that all her clothes were in the shop and had been sealed off, and now that the weather was cold, she was still wearing thin clothing, breaking down in tears as she spoke. Defendant Sun Maokun, accompanied by his defense lawyer, testified that Mrs. Sun had left without saying goodbye on the morning of August 17th. He claimed that he had previously borrowed money and organized a cooperative to sustain the shop. After Mrs. Sun left, various creditors came to demand repayment of debts, and the shop employees also demanded their wages. He was forced to close the shop. Later, eight creditors, including Dayou Factory, entrusted lawyer Wang Chengmo to post a notice of liquidation and filed a lawsuit in the Civil Court. He sent his younger brother, Sun Xiaofu, to search for Mrs. Sun with creditors Huang Shuncai and a Mr. Gao, but they could not find her. He then sold the shop, and the proceeds were held by the lawyer, not yet delivered to the creditors, and so on. When questioned, plaintiff Gong Sun denied fleeing, stating that she had returned to her hometown to commemorate the anniversary of her late husband's death. The defendant's younger brother, Sun Xiaofu, had come to her house with a fellow townsman to arrange a marriage, but he had not mentioned the shop's liquidation or sale. Furthermore, her husband had operated the shop for six years, earning thousands of yuan annually without any losses, and she had a seventy-year-old mother-in-law and children relying on the shop for their livelihood. The court noted the conflicting testimonies and ordered an investigation of the case and the summoning of witnesses, adjourning the hearing to 2:00 PM on the ninth for further examination of witnesses.

County Government Urges Increase in Tax on Reclaimed Land 105

Regarding the case of increasing the tax on reclaimed private land, the Shanghai County Government has ordered the Land Tax Collection Office to divide the area and prepare a register of reclaimed land, ordering the township chiefs to supervise the verification of the landowners cultivating the land according to the listed households, submit the deeds, old strings, and previous payment receipts, and register them for tax increase. The County Government received an order from the Finance Department stating that this case should be concluded by the end of this year. If concealed land without tax payment is discovered during the period, the land will be confiscated. In addition to the announcement issued by the County Government yesterday, it also notified the township chiefs and landowners that if the land is indeed unclaimed, they should submit a sworn statement for verification by personnel to be sent.

Mixing Counterfeit Money and Offering Bribes for Release: Chen Guilin Detained Awaiting Sentence 110

Chen Guilin from Jiangbei went to the Yanzhi paper store at 11799 Yangshupu Road the other day to try to pass a five-yuan counterfeit note from the Bank of China. The store owner, Mrs. Tang Huqin, caught him and called police officer 2250 who arrested him. Another five-yuan fake note from the Bank of Communications was found in his person. He was taken to the police station for detention, and the next morning, handed over to the First Special Court's Criminal Division Three. A lawyer for the Public Works Department, Zhang Shizhu, claimed that the defendant said in the police station that the counterfeit note had been given to him by a woman named Su Guiying who lived at 340 Rue Robert, to pay off a debt. Detectives had been sent to investigate, and while Su Guiying was confirmed to exist, she had moved a day before. A Chen Xiaosan claimed that he had never been given any such counterfeit money, and it was all a false accusation. Furthermore, after being arrested, the defendant had offered police officer 2250 one yuan in real money in an attempt to bribe his release. The eleven yuan in real and fake notes were submitted for examination. Chen Guilin's testimony was evasive. Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered him to be detained awaiting sentencing.

Wu Kang and Others Sentenced for Selling Opium 111

Chinese detective Jiang Linxiang raided an opium den at No. 9, Lane 448, Wuchang Road, at around 1:00 PM the other day, arresting the ringleader, Wu Kang from Guangdong, and confiscating a set of opium paraphernalia. The opium smokers, Hu Gongda, also from Guangdong, along with opium, copper coins, and silver coins, were taken to the Hongkou police station for detention. The next morning, they were handed over to the First Special District Court's Criminal Division Three. Public Works Department lawyer Zhang Shizhu presented the case and requested prosecution. Detective Jiang then reported the details of the raid, submitting the evidence. Judge Jiang questioned the two defendants and, upon clarifying the facts, sentenced Wu Kang to six months in prison and Hu Gongda to a fine of one hundred yuan. The evidence was confiscated.

Lodger Commits Suicide in Minhe Small Hotel 113

Zhuang Hongxing, a 21-year-old tailor from Haiyan, Zhejiang, checked into room No. 2 of the Minhe Small Hotel at 120 Rue Remi on the 1st of this month, paying the room fee. He then left and returned to the hotel to sleep at 8:00 PM. For some unknown reason, he committed suicide by swallowing raw opium. The next morning at 6:00 AM, the waiter entered the room to empty the chamber pot and saw nothing unusual. At 11:00 AM, the waiter urged him to get up, but there was no response. Only then did he discover that Zhuang had died in bed. He reported it to the Xuhui police station, which sent detectives to investigate. The body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan mortuary. Yesterday was a holiday, and it will be reported to the Second Special Court today for an autopsy.

Laundry Apprentice Run Over and Killed by Car 114

Jin Amao, a 37-year-old driver from Chuansha employed by Heyitai Coal Company at No. 853 Riyue Bridge East, Longhua Road, South Shanghai, was driving truck No. 227 loaded with coal to the city at noon on the 22nd of last month. While driving on the eight-mile bridge road, near the Ningbo Guild Hall in the French Concession, heading north and south, as he approached Ningbo Road, he tried to overtake a tram on the Fifth Road. At that moment, Mo Ruisheng, a 16-year-old apprentice from Shaoxing at the Nanhua Chang Laundry at No. 540, Republic Road, was walking there and suddenly angled northwest into the road, where he was hit and run over by Jin Amao's coal truck, resulting in fatal injuries and instant death. The police arrested Jin and sent the body to the morgue for examination, reporting it to the court. The police attorney charged Jin with causing death through negligence. Jin hired lawyer Lin Yingqing for his defense. Details of the case have been reported in this newspaper. The case has been concluded by Judge Xiong Huiping of the Second Special Court, who yesterday sentenced Jin Amao to three years in prison for causing death through negligence in his profession and ordered him to be transferred to the detention center during the appeal period. It is reported that the defendant's side, after receiving the verdict, decided to appeal to the High Court Third Branch.

Publication of Allegorical Novel "The Extraordinary Adventures of a Beauty": The China Bookstore at 193 Aiwenyi Road, Datong Road, this port, after months of preparation, is scheduled to open today. It is said that the bookstore specializes in printing books beneficial to society and the country. The first publication is the allegorical novel and patriotic book "The Extraordinary Adventures of a Beauty." It is said that during Japan's time of poverty and weakness, amidst internal and external troubles, this book was fortunate to be published, and people from all walks of life eagerly read it and were deeply moved, which promoted the Meiji Restoration. Mr. Liang Qichao once said in his "Yinbingshi Wenji" that the reason for Japan's wealth and strength lies in "The Extraordinary Adventures of a Beauty." Thus, the potential and moving power of this book can be imagined. The content of this book mainly focuses on talented scholars and beauties, but all the narratives concern the rise and fall of countries in the world, their strengths and weaknesses, advantages and disadvantages, and their causes. It can awaken weak nations and make them aware of the difference between strength and demise, understand the principles of natural selection, and eliminate numb and bad mentalities, replacing them with conscience and responsibility. The bookstore believes that this book can indeed benefit the national economy and the people's livelihood, and after a long period of time, it has been translated into Chinese and is now published.

Descendants of the Jian'an Liu Clan Reprint "The Record of Loyalty" and "The Collected Works of Pingshan": The two books "The Record of Loyalty of the Jian'an Liu Clan" and "The Collected Works of Pingshan" have been around for a long time, and genuine copies of each book are rare, so they are not easy to purchase. Scholars who study the principles regard them as treasures. Recently, Mr. Wenzao and Mr. Yongkang, descendants of the Liu clan of Jinshan, reprinted the books to promote the virtues of their ancestors and benefit scholars, which is truly rare. The original price of the two books, sold at Xing Sheng Street in the French Concession of this port by Jiang Xingchang Xing Shen Tai two woolen shops is one dollar and one dollar and fifty cents, respectively. It is said that half of the proceeds will be used for flood relief donations, and half will be used to cover costs.

Publication of "The Collected Works of Tan Youxia": The Poems and Essays of a Master of the Jingling School in the Late Ming Dynasty 121

Mr. Zhou Zuoren's lecture on the New Literature Movement traces its origins to the Gong'an and Jingling schools of the late Ming Dynasty. Scholars across the country have been studying the literature of the late Ming Dynasty, and there have been new discoveries in the past two years. However, the literary works of the Gong'an and Jingling schools were banned and destroyed during the Qing Dynasty, and they are not widely circulated. Private collections are regarded as treasures and are not easy to obtain. The Shanghai Magazine Company is now publishing the "Rare Chinese Literature Series." In addition to Song Ci and Yuan Qu, the series emphasizes the late Ming Dynasty in terms of literary collections, and the poems and essays of the five masters of the Gong'an and Jingling schools—the three Yuan brothers, Zhong Xing, and Tan Yuanchun—are all included in the first collection. Yuan Xiaoxiu's diary has already been published and has been reprinted. Last week, the 8th issue specially published "The Collected Works of Tan Youxia," a master of the Jingling school, based on the original Ming Dynasty edition of twenty-three volumes, which has been completely copied and supplemented by Shen Qihou at the Beiping Library. It is truly a rare and precious literary collection. Those who love literature and study the origins of the literature of the late Ming Dynasty and the New Literature Movement must read the works of this Jingling master. Loose copies are sold at a popular price of fifty cents, and special printed copies are sold at seventy cents, with a free paper cover. Direct retail sales offer a 10% discount, and out-of-town mail orders are exempt from postage.

A Visit to the Free Farm 124

— Jinhua Ting

From Here You Can Understand the History and Quality of Milk

In recent years, milk has occupied a very large place among the foods in our country. Taking Shanghai as an example, whether it is Western restaurants, biscuit factories, or major hotels, clubs, and entertainment venues, they all use a large amount of milk every day. At the same time, ordinary families directly order milk from various milk companies, which probably accounts for more than 60% of the city's daily milk production of more than 30,000 pounds. From this point of view, the wide range of uses of milk is undisputed. However, most people only know that milk is a food rich in nutrients and beneficial to the body, but most people do not understand the whole process of milk production and the quality of milk. As for what kind of milk is called A-grade milk, what kind of milk is called B-grade milk, and what are the ingredients contained in milk, whether it is pure or not, what are the benefits of eating sterilized milk to the human body, and what are the harms of eating unsterilized milk to the human body, because there are already many milk factories in Shanghai, among which many meet the inspection regulations of the Public Works Department and the Municipal Health Bureau, but there are also quite a few that do not meet the inspection regulations or even have not been inspected. If you are not careful and eat inferior milk, it is not only useless but also harmful. Because of this reason, the reporter made a special trip to the Free Farm, which has a good reputation and the best performance, for an inspection. Now I will record the various situations obtained from the inspection in detail below.

A Tour of the Whole Farm

Our group of seven people arrived at the Free Farm on Kang Nao Tu Road at 3:30 PM that afternoon. Mr. You Huaihao, the head of the farm, and Mr. Shen Guotang, the director of the "Family Service Society" founded by the farm, received us very warmly. For the sake of easy understanding and saving time, we first took a tour of the whole farm.

1. Cow Shed: The entire shed has 120 dairy cows. The farm is rectangular in shape. The middle is the aisle. On the left and right sides of the aisle, there are four rows of iron fences. Each grid tethers a cow. Although these cows are tethered in each grid, they can still move forward and backward freely. The two sides are feeding lanes. Feeding is done three times a day, at 7:00 AM, 2:00 PM, and 10:00 PM. Milking is done at the same time as feeding, so milking is also done three times a day. The cow workers are divided into groups of six, with four skilled workers and two assistants in each group, managing a total of 40 dairy cows. Another person specializes in measuring the temperature of the cows and checking for diseases, and another person specializes in managing the feed. The entire shed is supervised by a foreman to supervise and manage the workers. Mr. You said that the construction of the cow shed has certain dimensions. The most important thing is that the entire site should be three inches higher than the street surface outside the farm, and the cow shed should be six inches higher than the entire site, so that all the water can flow out easily and not accumulate. The total width of the cow shed is 34 feet. Other dimensions, such as the cow stalls, aisles, feeding lanes, and waterways, all have certain dimensions. Windows and doors are used on both sides of the shed and on the roof to allow air circulation and bright light. There are many types of dairy cows in the world, but the following four types are the best in terms of production and nutrients.

(A) Holstein Cattle: Holstein cattle have the longest history among dairy cows. They have been spread in Europe for a thousand years. The place of origin is Holland. Now, milk farms in Belgium, Holland, Germany, the United States, and other countries all have their traces. Their bodies are black and white, and they are very large. The average weight is about 1,300 pounds, and some are 1,500 to 1,700 pounds. They are very docile. The milk production is higher than any other type of dairy cow, but the fat content is very low, and the oil globules are also small, making oil extraction more difficult. However, they have a lot of protein, making them the best for feeding children.

(B) Jersey Cattle: According to research, Jersey dairy cows originated in Switzerland and are an excellent representative of dairy cows in southern Europe. These cows are now found all over the world. Each one weighs about 900 pounds, and males weigh 1,300 to 700 pounds. They are very docile. The milk they produce usually contains 5.5% fat, and sometimes even 6% to 7%. One pound of butter can be extracted from 16 to 19 pounds of milk, and the oil globules are very large, making oil extraction easier. These cows are considered the most refined among dairy cows.

(C) Guernsey Cattle: Guernsey cattle were brought from Guernsey Island in Holland. In the past, they were only used by nobles in Europe, so they were not very popular. Now, there are very many Guernsey cattle farms in the United States. Guernsey cattle are plumper than Jersey cattle, weighing about 1,050 pounds to 1,250 pounds. They are very cold-resistant and very intelligent. Their milk production is more than Jersey, but the butter content is not as high as Jersey. These cows can produce 6,000 to 9,000 pounds of milk per year.

(D) Ayrshire Cattle: Ayrshire dairy cows have the best appearance, but they are the youngest in the history of selection. In the 18th century, some farmers in Ayrshire, Scotland, disliked them for being too small and thin, and their milk production was also low. They transported some other breeds from the Netherlands to mix, and as a result, they selected Ayrshire dairy cows. The dairy cows weigh about 1,000 pounds, and the male cows weigh about 1,500 pounds. Because they were improved from wild species, and the years are not many, they are very temperamental, so they are difficult to serve. These cows are currently still undergoing precise selection and improvement, so the milk production is not as much as other types.

The Free Farm has three types of dairy cows: the first type is Holstein, the second type is Jersey, and the third type is non-purebred. According to Mr. You, these three types of dairy cows are all foreign breeds, some bought from the United States, some bought from Canada, and some grown locally. The purchase price of each cow is about 500 to 700 yuan (national currency). Among the three types of dairy cows, Holstein has the highest production, and Jersey has the most fat. The total production of the entire farm is 1,600 to 1,800 pounds per day in winter and spring, and 1,000 to 1,200 pounds per day in summer and autumn.

2. Bottle Washing Department: After passing through the refrigeration department from the cow shed, we turned to the bottle washing department. Bottle washing is a very important part of the work in a milk factory. All used milk bottles must be washed three times and go through four steps. The first step is to wash away the oily dirt, the second step is to put the bottles on the machine to wipe off the oil stains inside and outside, the third step is to wash them clean, and the fourth step is to send the washed milk bottles to the steam room and cook them at a temperature of 200 degrees Fahrenheit for 15 minutes, and then send them to the bottle filling department next door. In addition, the large and small lead buckets used to hold milk must also be washed and boiled in the same way, and these lead buckets are all made of original lead quality and have no seams to prevent other dirty things from entering.

3. Sterilization Department: Finally, we arrived at the sterilization department. The work in this department is the most important. There is a milk boiling pot in the center. In front of the pot, there is a cooling milk machine with different gears. After the milk is squeezed from the dairy cows, it is transported to the sterilization room in the above-mentioned lead buckets and poured into the milk pot to let it boil. It is most suitable to cook it to 145 degrees Fahrenheit, and at most to 148.5 degrees. The time is 30 minutes. If it does not reach this temperature, the "E. coli" in the milk cannot be completely eliminated. If it exceeds this temperature, the "vitamin," also known as "vitamin," in the half-milk will be affected, and the nutritional content of this milk will be reduced. Therefore, an "automatic recording thermometer" must be set up in this room. Each day, an automatic recording form is used to indicate whether the milk has been heated to 145 degrees and whether it has been heated for 30 minutes. The milk is transferred from the sterilizer to the cooling milk machine using a pump. The cooling milk machine is flat, so that when the milk passes through the tube, it is successful in a very thin range. The milk is cooled to 45 degrees, and then the milk is poured into bottles using a bottling machine and sealed by hand. Because the sealing is done by machine, the worker's fingers absolutely cannot come into contact with the milk. Finally, it is sent to the cold storage room to gradually lower the temperature of the milk, so that the milk microorganisms in the milk will not develop and survive. Elimination of Inferior Milk: The milk industry has made great progress in recent years, which should be attributed to the Public Works Department, because without its promotion and advancement, it would probably not be possible to obtain this good milk today, because eight years ago the milk industry was extremely immature, and today's milk industry has become a scientific milk industry.

2. The Difference Between "A" Grade Milk and "B" Grade Milk: In terms of the ingredients of milk, A grade and B grade are the same. The difference lies entirely in the issue of pure hygiene. Therefore, A grade milk, first, must have complete sanitary equipment; second, it must have technically astute management talent and well-trained work assistants; and third, it must have the close supervision and guidance of the competent authority. All three are indispensable, because without equipment, it is impossible to produce qualified A grade milk. For example, with steam equipment, it is possible to sterilize the milk itself and the utensils and equipment that come into contact with the milk. With refrigeration equipment, the bacteria in the milk can be prevented from developing and fermenting and spoiling. But with equipment, without the corresponding technical talent to use it, this equipment is also useless. But with equipment and talent, without the so-called competent authority to supervise and inspect, it is also useless, because bacteria are invisible to the naked eye and must be known after a chemical test of the milk's content. This is the most important part of the work. After inspection, the qualification of A grade milk can be determined. Therefore, A grade milk has been medically tested by the competent authority, and B grade milk has not been tested. So A grade milk can be drunk cold, and B grade milk is not safe to drink cold.

3. Three Different Inspection Works

A. Inspection of Milk Farms: To make milk popular and sold in Shanghai, it is necessary to obtain a license from the three health bureaus. The Public Concession Health Department has 30 rules, the disinfection rules have 9 articles, and the Municipal Health Bureau and the French Concession Health Bureau each have 19 articles. All matters concerning the cleanliness of the environment and dairy cows, the construction of houses, the smoothness of ditches, the equipment of machines, whether the work is legal, whether the water is safe, and the health of the workers are included. Approximately for historical reasons, the Public Concession Health Department is in the leading position, and most of the work is handled by the Health Department. Health workers often work day and night and are responsible for this inspection work, but in the near future, it is feared that the milk companies in the Chinese area will be fully inspected by the Municipal Health Bureau. It is heard that one or two milk or goat milk companies, which were previously managed by the Health Department, have now abandoned this responsibility and are now under the Municipal Health Bureau.

Expert Talks

After we finished the tour of the whole farm, we returned to the reception room. They politely prepared milk, black tea, and various delicacies, as well as their own milk cakes, which were very delicious. After we had tea and snacks, Mr. You began to talk about the technical aspects of milk.

1. Types of Milk Grading in Shanghai: Although milk in Shanghai is divided into A and B grades, there are four different types: one is A grade sterilized, the second is B grade unsterilized, the third is A grade unsterilized, and the fourth is B grade unsterilized. This grading method has only been implemented for eight years and was formulated by the Health Department of the Public Works Department. It is a policy to encourage the improvement of the milk industry, so that the superior can survive,

(B) Inspection of Dairy Cows: There are two types of dairy cow inspections: one is a regular general inspection, and the other is a tuberculosis inspection, both of which are handled by the Public Concession Health Department and do not charge any fees. Dairy cows of A grade milk companies are inspected once every three months, and dairy cows of B grade milk companies are inspected once every six months. If tuberculosis is found in the Shanghai dairy cows, the dairy cow will be ordered to be slaughtered without any leniency, because tuberculosis in the lungs is not easy to spread, while tuberculosis in the mammary glands will be transmitted to the milk. Tuberculosis was not inspected before. Since 1928, because Dr. Wang Zhaoqi, a veterinarian from the Shanghai Municipal Government Health Bureau, wanted to handle the inspection procedures, the Public Works Department hired Dr. Shu Shubei, a veterinarian who studied at Cornell University, to implement the inspection of dairy cows without charging any fees. Since then, Shanghai's milk industry has greatly improved, but the results after the inspection were shocking. It was only then that it was known that 50% to 80% of the dairy cows in Shanghai had tuberculosis. To remedy this shortcoming, on the one hand, efforts were made to gradually reduce the number of tuberculosis cows, and on the other hand, all the milk was sterilized, because there was no problem after sterilization. Therefore, regarding B grade milk, the Public Works Department initiated the joint organization of a central milk sterilization plant last year, in order to sterilize all B grade milk to ensure the safety of citizens drinking milk. Later, due to various reasons, it did not succeed. The Public Works Department, in order to consistently implement its proposition that milk must be sterilized, re-stipulated that all B grade milk in Shanghai must be sterilized by June 30, 1936, otherwise they will be ordered to stop business. This is the situation in the British Concession. The Chinese and French Concessions are also conducting inspection work at the same time.

(C) Inspection of Milk: There are also two different inspections of milk: (1) inspection of ingredients. It is of course true that the milk does not contain E. coli and will not cause illness, but whether it has obtained the nourishment of milk is still a problem. In relatively advanced cities in Shanghai, there are of course health authorities who send personnel to inspect whether the milk farms are legal and whether the milk meets the regulations. Under such circumstances, there is of course no need to worry. But look at the current domestic situation, how many places have established health authorities to manage these things, then we pay the price and order milk, and we should also know whether it is reliable or not, and whether it is hygienic or not. To understand these questions, we must first clarify the original ingredients of milk, and then see if there will be chemical changes after adding other things. Milk contains four major elements, and its composition is as follows:

(1) Water accounts for about 88%

(2) Fat (i.e. butter) accounts for about 4%

(3) Protein, etc. accounts for about 8%

(4) Minerals or carbonaceous matter accounts for about 0.9%

Under the management of the Public Works Department Health Department, the layer of water is not a problem, so what should be paid attention to when drinking milk is a kind of microorganism invisible to the naked eye. As for the ordinary use of a milk meter to measure the ingredients of milk, it must be accurate when the milk temperature is 60 degrees, otherwise the milk temperature will be too high, and the milk meter will float. Two, is the inspection of bacteria, there are two kinds of bacteria to be inspected in milk, the first is milk bacteria, it is stipulated that each CC should not exceed the ordinary reading of ten thousand, (this is the A grade non-sterilized milk regulation) after sterilization, each CC should not exceed 30,000, (this is the A grade sterilized milk regulation) the second kind is fecal bacteria, that is, standard bacteria, also known as E. coli, it is used to measure the existence of various germs, it is stipulated that this bacteria cannot be found in one tenth CC, if it is found, the Public Works Department will issue a standard warning letter for the first time, and at the same time order an investigation and improvement, if the root cause is not immediately investigated and intentionally committed several times, the Public Works Department has the right to temporarily cancel the A grade milk license, if the milk is adulterated with water, the Public Works Department will file a public prosecution and punish it, if it is not improved and often violates regulations, the license will be revoked and the business will be stopped,

Because pulmonary tuberculosis dairy cows cannot be eliminated, there is a danger of spreading the disease in contact with the air, so the benefits of sterilization and the harms of non-sterilization are obvious. Then the quality of milk is not entirely in the concentration of the quality, because under the management of the Public Works Department, the problem of adulteration with water has become a thing of the past and will never happen, and the invisible bacteria in milk that make people sick are a very big problem, so to make milk pure, safe, and hygienic, it is a product of the combination of equipment, talent, and inspection, and one is indispensable. (To be continued)

Regulations for the Organization of Labor Education Committees in Various Cities and Counties Jointly Promulgated by the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry

The Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry jointly promulgated the following regulations on the organization of labor education committees in various cities and counties: (Article 1) The provincial government shall order cities and counties with developed industries in each province to organize their respective labor education committees in accordance with these regulations, which shall be subordinate to the Executive Yuan; cities under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan shall organize their respective labor education committees in accordance with these regulations. (Article 2) The competent authorities referred to in these regulations shall be the municipal government in cities, the county government in counties, and the Bureau of Social Affairs and the Bureau of Education in cities under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan. (Article 3) The purpose of the labor education committees in various cities and counties shall be to study and promote the implementation of local labor education. (Article 4) The labor education committees in various cities and counties shall have seven to nine members, who shall be appointed from the following personnel: (1) Two competent officials dispatched by the competent authorities; (2) Two people hired by the competent authorities from labor and capital organizations; (3) Three to five people hired by the competent authorities from local social welfare organizations and people who are enthusiastic about labor education. (Article 5) Each labor education committee in each city and county shall have one chairman and one vice-chairman, who shall be appointed by the members dispatched by the competent authorities. (Article 6) The members of the labor education committees in each city and county shall serve in honorary positions. (Article 7) The labor education committees in each city and county shall, under the command of the competent authorities, handle the following matters: (1) Matters related to the research and guidance of the implementation of labor education; (2) Matters related to the planning, assistance, and promotion of labor education; (3) Matters related to the investigation and statistics of the status of labor education and out-of-school laborers; (4) Matters related to the propaganda and compilation of labor education materials; (5) Labor education matters submitted for discussion by the competent authorities; (6) Other matters related to labor education. (Article 8) The resolutions of the labor education committees in each city and county shall be submitted to the competent authorities for approval before implementation. (Article 9) The labor education committees in each county and county may appoint several staff members, who shall be concurrently appointed by the competent authorities from among their subordinate staff. (Article 10) The labor education committees in each city and county shall hold a meeting once a month, and temporary meetings may be convened by the chairman when necessary. (Article 12) The labor education committees in each city and county shall prepare a work report every six months and submit it to the competent authorities for submission to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Education for record. (Article 12) The labor education committees in each city and county may formulate detailed rules of procedure and rules of procedure for meetings in accordance with these regulations, and submit them to the competent authorities for approval. (Article 13) These regulations shall not apply to the labor education experiment areas designated by the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Education. (Article 14) Any matters not covered by these regulations shall be jointly amended by the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Education. (Article 15) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Guizhou Department of Education Subsidizes Guizhou Students in Various Universities – Forty Provincial-Funded Subsidy Students Established – Notices Sent to Various Universities for Notification

The Guizhou Provincial Department of Education recently sent a letter to universities in this port and domestic universities, stating that the regulations for provincial-funded subsidy students from this province in domestic universities have been revised by this department and submitted to the 178th regular meeting of the Guizhou Provincial Government Committee for approval and promulgation. In the future, the application for subsidy fees for Guizhou students in domestic universities shall be handled in accordance with these regulations. Correspondingly, ten copies each of the Guizhou Provincial Department of Education's regulations for provincial-funded subsidy students in domestic universities, application forms, resumes, and grade reports are enclosed for reference, and it is hoped that Guizhou students will be notified to comply with them. The attached regulations are as follows:

(1) In order to cultivate specialized talents in this province, forty places for provincial-funded subsidy students are specially established to encourage advancement.

(2) Provincial-funded subsidy students in this province shall be limited to studying in departments of science, engineering, agriculture, medicine, and education in national universities and the following public and private universities: A. Nanjing Jinling University, B. Wuxi Jiangsu Provincial Institute of Education, C. Peking Yenching University, Peking Union Medical College, D. Tianjin Nankai University, E. Changsha Xiangya Medical College, F. Wuzhou Guangxi University.

(3) Graduates from secondary schools in this province who have been admitted to universities and departments that meet the requirements of the preceding article and have completed one year of study with grades of B or above, and have been certified by the school, may apply for subsidies in accordance with the prescribed procedures.

(4) All applicants for provincial-funded subsidies shall fill out the application form, resume, certificate of study from the school, and certificate of grades from the professor in charge, and send them together with a four-inch half-length photo to the school for submission to the Department of Education for verification.

(5) If the number of provincial-funded subsidy students approved by the Department of Education exceeds the quota, the Department of Education shall register and fill the vacancies in the following order: A. Those with better grades listed on the grade report shall be filled first; B. If the grades are equal, those in higher grades shall be filled first; C. If the grades and grades are equal, they shall be filled in the order of registration.

(6) The subsidy fee for each student in this province shall be 200 yuan per year, which shall be sent in two installments by the school for the student to receive.

(7) The subsidy period shall be from the date of approval to the predetermined graduation year of the student.

(8) Provincial-funded subsidy students shall submit a grade report every semester, and shall submit a graduation certificate and a graduation thesis after graduation.

(9) Provincial-funded subsidy students who are about to complete the subsidy period and have special circumstances that require continued application for subsidy shall submit a detailed report of the reasons and attach supporting documents one semester in advance and submit it to the school for submission to the Department of Education for verification.

(10) The subsidy for provincial-funded subsidy students may be terminated at any time if any of the following occurs: A. Improper behavior, B. Arbitrary changes to the school or department, C. Poor grades or failing grades for two consecutive semesters.

(11) These regulations shall be promulgated and implemented after being approved by the Guizhou Provincial Government Committee and shall be submitted to the Ministry of Education for record.

Shanghai Branch of the Educational Film Association Revises the Method of Rotating Educational Films – Twice per School per Semester, Six Reels Each Time – Has Been Approved by the Municipal Education Bureau for Implementation

The Shanghai Branch of the China Educational Film Association has been praised by various schools since it was approved by the Ministry of Education to rotate educational films in schools at all levels in this city. There are currently a total of 152 schools in this city that charge low fees. It was originally planned to show films three times per school per semester, with four reels per show. With one set of projectors rotating, showing four schools per day, it would take about one and a half months to show all 152 schools per week, excluding Sundays. It was also often inconvenient due to temporary events at schools that changed the time, which would inevitably affect other schools. Therefore, a new method has been formulated, changing the showing to once per school per semester, with six reels per show. This has been approved by the Education Bureau for implementation. The revised method is as follows: (1) In order to avoid errors in mailing, the Shanghai Branch will post the schedule of school names and times for the next week (Monday to Sunday) in the newspaper's public announcement column every Saturday, starting from October 4, 1935, without separate notification. (2) If a school with a scheduled showing needs to change the showing time, it can cut out the school exchange time change notification form attached to the newspaper within two days from the date of publication, fill it out clearly, and send it to the association. The association will reallocate it according to the situation and notify the school. (3) If the Shanghai Branch's staff arrives at the school on time for the showing, but the school does not show the film, it will be considered as having been shown. This does not apply to outdoor showings that cannot be held due to rain. (4) Each time the Shanghai Branch's staff arrives at the school to show the film, they will bring a consultation form to be filled out and stamped by the school for future reference. (5) Starting from the second semester of 1935, the Shanghai Branch will send the names of the films and their descriptions to each school for students to announce before each rotation week. (6) If a school needs to prepare a black cloth, it must send someone to the association to pick it up before the showing and return it immediately after the showing to avoid affecting other schools' borrowing.

Economic Supplement: The Inside Story of the Soaring Gold Price and Its Causes and Consequences by Zhang Yifan

"1"

The monetary system that is stuck in the metal standard rut attempts to establish a permanent and unchanging measure of value, or at least a relatively stable one. The slim hope for this and the minimal possibility have long been proven by the fact that precious metal prices rise and fall drastically.

If people are used to using gold, and therefore must try to create a new currency that can truly serve as a measure of value based on this habit, this situation is really like a person who is stuck in a muddy puddle. Instead of thinking about climbing ashore (jumping ashore is actually impossible, so one can only think about climbing ashore), he struggles hard in the same place, trying to extricate himself. As a result, there is no other harvest to hope for except for going further and further down and dying.

Isn't that so? The trend of high gold prices and low silver prices was only like the day before yesterday. And today's trend of high silver prices and low gold prices is about to become yesterday's event. The current sharp drop in China's exchange rate and the surge in gold prices in Shanghai are descending like a storm.

During the period of high gold prices and low silver prices, everyone deeply felt the soaring prices at that time, the increasing burden of life, the high prices of various advanced means of production, and the great losses in international balance of payments. Therefore, they strongly advocated banning the export of gold, or advocated gradually adopting the gold standard system. They all agreed that only in this way could modern production technology be used to revitalize domestic industries as much as possible, reduce the people's burden of living to enrich the society and the country, and at the same time, avoid this kind of unwarranted loss in international balance of payments.

Although this plan was not realized, it was actually fortunate that it was not realized. However, the hope for a renewed collapse in gold prices was immediately realized after only a short two years. However, because this time the drop in gold prices was excessive and the rise in silver prices was too great, domestic silver was exported one after another, and financial panic broke out in various places as credit tightened sharply. At the same time, prices fell in the opposite direction, and nine out of ten producers suffered losses. Therefore, the whole country was alarmed, and they strongly advocated banning the export of silver, devaluing the currency, and proposing various countermeasures that lingered on the metal standard. Some have in fact been realized, and some are in fact preparing to be realized. At this time, everyone thought that only in this way could prices rise and industries be maintained. Therefore, looking back, they not only no longer felt the harm of the trend of high gold prices and low silver prices in the twentieth year of the Republic, but almost unanimously believed that only low silver prices and high gold prices "can enable China to avoid the economic panic that has spread around the world," and even pointed out that the time was "a period of prosperity for China."

This contradictory feeling phenomenon can be said to be due to the fact that China's currency does not have a central policy, or that it is only caused by each person planning for his own subjective interests.

The group of people who are dissatisfied with high gold prices and low silver prices are mainly the comprador class, the fashionable friends, and the institutions with heavy foreign debts, because high gold prices and low silver prices lead to a sharp drop in foreign exchange rates, and the price of imported goods rises sharply, which greatly hits the comprador business. Therefore, ordinary fashionable friends cannot fully enjoy "modern material civilization." At the same time, repaying foreign debts requires spending more silver coins to meet the debts settled in gold prices, so they deeply feel the panic of insufficient income and expenditure.

However, when the opposite situation of high silver prices and low gold prices arrives, the people who are dissatisfied with this change to another group of people, mainly the gold sub-capital and industrial capital, and financial capital among silver standard countries. The main thing that represents their wealth is the price of silver. As a rule, expensive silver prices increase their wealth and invisibly increase their profits. But the pity is that most of the domestic silver is in the hands of foreign banks in China. Seeing that the overseas silver price is higher than that in China, for their own interests, they will inevitably transport the cash for export to seek the difference. Once the momentum of cash outflow is great, the domestic currency will suddenly tighten, and then the credit in various places will be extremely tight, and the industries will be declared bankrupt, and the national financial capital will suffer a double blow. The first is the threat of inflation, fearing that once inflation occurs, foreign banks will take the opportunity to oppress Chinese banks; the second is the impact of industrial bankruptcy, making it impossible for them to recover the principal and interest of the loans they have issued. Industrial capital suffers even greater blows; first, the soaring exchange rate causes import prices to be low and export prices to rise, which strengthens the economic pressure of international capitalists; second, the domestic wholesale price calculated in silver falls relatively, which reduces his profits and also risks losing his costs. Third, cash outflows in various places and tight credit lead to short-term chips and make it difficult to make further development plans, and even maintaining the status quo is worrying!

However, the majority of agricultural producers and the working masses, who account for the largest proportion of the total national population, suffer unwarranted disasters regardless of whether gold prices are high and silver prices are low or silver prices are high and gold prices are low. During the period of high gold prices and low silver prices, the collapse of export prices of agricultural products invisibly reduced his income; with the rising trend of domestic prices, agricultural products were slower than industrial products, and this scissor gap aggravated his pain in income and expenditure. Under the opposite phenomenon of high silver prices and low gold prices, in addition to the tariff barriers of various countries, devaluation and dumping are also implemented, and the state bears the responsibility for its losses. Therefore, the agricultural products in my country, which have increased export prices, have lost a corner of the overseas surplus market and are running into walls everywhere. At the same time, the collapse of domestic prices, the decline of agricultural products is more violent than that of industrial products, so the impact on farmers is more severe than others. Recently, there have been many great theories and famous works explaining that the economic panic in China today is due to the soaring and plummeting of silver prices, although it is inevitable to obliterate other causes, it cannot be denied the importance of its relationship.

As for the working masses, salaried classes, and self-employed people in cities, they have not felt the personal pain of "rice is as precious as pearls, firewood is as expensive as cinnamon, and life is difficult" in the situation of high gold prices and low silver prices. Because at that time, prices were raised, but the income of wages and salaries still stood still at a low level. On the contrary, in the situation of high silver prices and low gold prices, the burden of life is relatively reduced, but the real wage is also reduced at the same time. In particular, the bankruptcy of industries makes it impossible for them to maintain their livelihood occupations, and they join the ranks of the unemployed, so even if prices fall, it still has nothing to do with them.

Taking a step back, no matter whether gold prices are high and silver prices are low, or silver prices are low and gold prices are high, it can always give a considerable benefit to some people. But the pity is that the fate of this benefit is controlled by the hands of others, we can only float and sink with others, and be arranged by others. Looking at the current national horror under the high silver prices and low gold prices, in just the most recent week, the Shanghai gold standard and foreign exchange market prices have reversed the past phenomenon. Yesterday (October 30) the Shanghai gold standard market price has opened up the highest price that has never existed since ancient times, and each tael is worth as much as 1,183 yuan. Compared with the previous 1,000 yuan or so before the United States implemented the silver purchase policy, it is not the same, and it is

(Chlorine Water) Wash your hands once in it. A basin of chlorine water is placed at the entrance of the delivery room. In two years, the mortality rate of women in the first delivery room dropped from four hundred and fifty-nine to forty-five. Then, Ignaz's invention would probably be warmly welcomed. On the contrary, the professors of obstetrics at that time regarded his opinions as heresy. They said, "What? Is puerperal fever caused by our own hands as doctors? Absurd! Irrelevant!" In their minds, childbirth is naturally dangerous, and puerperal fever is an unavoidable disease. (4) Parasitic Stomatitis

Parasitic stomatitis is also known as thrush. It is caused by the transmission of a kind of thrush bacteria. Part of this bacteria is filamentous. Part of it is composed of circular spores. Its transmission route can be transmitted to the oral cavity through the medium of air, or it can parasitize on the feeding bottle and invade the mouth of the infant. This bacteria can especially develop and proliferate in the case of unclean oral cavity, decomposition of milk remaining in the oral cavity, dryness, and inflammation. Infants are most likely to develop this disease (most common in infants one or two weeks after birth). In adults, it often occurs in patients with severe typhoid fever, pulmonary tuberculosis, cancer, diabetes, and other debilitating conditions.

The main symptoms of thrush are redness, swelling, and white patches on the mucous membrane of the tongue, cheeks, and soft palate. The white patches are initially small, then gradually enlarge. The inner surface of the oral cavity appears white, like snow, so it is commonly called "snow mouth." In the early stage, it can be easily peeled off, but in the later stage, it is often fixed and appears yellowish or reddish-brown. Sometimes the white patches can even spread to the pharynx, throat, and esophagus. Saliva secretion is mostly vigorous. Infants often feel inconvenience and pain when breastfeeding, which often causes crying. Sometimes there are also symptoms such as diarrhea and emaciation. Adults also often complain of pain when chewing and swallowing. The course of this disease is about one to two weeks. Its treatment should first focus on oral hygiene. Before and after breastfeeding, infants should use 2% boric acid solution to clean the oral cavity at all times. At the same time, the mother's nipples and feeding bottles should also be kept clean. If white patches have already appeared in the oral cavity, use a medicated solution that inhibits the growth of bacteria to apply or gargle.

(5) Gangrenous Stomatitis

Gangrenous stomatitis is also known as water cancer. It is one of the most dangerous types of stomatitis. It is more common in children with weak constitutions. Its predisposing factors can be divided into two types: internal and external. External factors include poverty, malnutrition, and lack of cleanliness. Internal factors include infectious diseases such as measles, scarlet fever, pertussis, smallpox, intermittent fever, pneumonia, dysentery, tuberculosis, syphilis, and systemic diseases such as Meleney's ulcer, hemorrhagic diathesis, etc. Clinically, it is more common to occur secondary to measles.

The main symptom of this disease is the appearance of blisters on the mucous membrane of the cheeks (near the corners of the mouth), followed by ulcers. Its putrid odor is offensive. The spread from the lesion to the surface and deep tissues is very rapid. Therefore, in just a few days, the infiltration can reach the outside of the cheeks, and the ulcer breaks through to the outside, exposing the bone, which soon dies. Therefore, the appearance of this disease is indeed cheek gangrene. At the same time, the affected side of the face also develops collateral edema. The nearby lymph nodes also become swollen. Furthermore, this disease often causes high fever, often reaching around 40 degrees Celsius. The consumption of physical strength is also very rapid. Patients feel local pain. Saliva secretion is also vigorous and mixed with purulent blood.

The prognosis of this disease is very poor. It is more likely to be fatal than to recover. Its mortality rate is about three-quarters. The cause of death may be sudden collapse or weakness after the illness. The treatment method is to use cauterization or corrosion to prevent the spread of the lesion. On the one hand, pay attention to the patient's nutrition and try to maintain his physical strength, but in most cases, death is inevitable. A Brief Discussion on Pulmonary Tuberculosis (73) Hu Jiayan

Section 3 Mental Cultivation of the Patient

Regarding dietary taboos as a treatment method, a considerable number of people have advocated it recently; they believe that reducing the amount of chlorine伊洪 in the body has the effect of accelerating the formation of connective tissue. Their argument is: restrict the patient's salt intake. If there is a loss of appetite, other spices or meat juices can be used as substitutes; meat should also be limited, water intake should be reduced, and fat intake can be increased. Fresh vegetables and fruits can also be increased in large quantities. This treatment method has the best results for skin tuberculosis and also provides some assistance for pulmonary tuberculosis; however, there is still no conclusion as to which stage or type is most suitable, and this can only be corrected by those who come later!

The importance of quiet rest in the treatment of this disease has already been discussed above: but relying solely on this kind of physical quietness is sometimes not enough, so whether the patient's mental state is quiet or not is also a major issue in treatment and is worth emphasizing. We must understand that the emotions of pulmonary tuberculosis patients are mostly excessively sensitive; even if he closes his eyes and lies down all day, his mental activities will not stop. He pays close attention to the details of his daily symptoms: such as the presence or absence of cough, the level of body temperature, the presence or absence of tubercle bacilli in the sputum, and the goodness or badness of appetite, etc., without being bothered by the trivialities. Therefore, although the body is quiet, the mind is not quiet, which is of course harmful and not beneficial to the progress of the disease. If the symptoms show slight changes, such as a higher temperature or a poor appetite; sometimes these are just temporary gains and losses and have nothing to do with the overall situation, but the patient feels depressed and inexplicably upset, thinking that the disease has deteriorated! Even if the doctor tries his best to comfort him, he cannot relieve the depression in his heart. As a result, he falls into severe neurasthenia, and the patient's self-confidence and courage are lost. Often, diseases that can be cured end up being unmanageable: truly, "a trickle not stopped will eventually become a river!"

(Question 43) What is the function of dental pulp?

(Answer) There are two functions: (1) To produce and nourish the dentin. If the dentin is damaged, it will regenerate a layer of dentin to protect itself, which is called secondary dentin. (2) It is rich in sensation and can respond to external stimuli such as cold, heat, chemical, or mechanical stimulation.

(Question 44) How does the dental pulp sense external stimuli? What are the benefits of this response?

(Answer) Its response is pain. For example, if we eat something too cold, too hot, or too sour, our teeth will feel sore and painful. Or if the teeth are hit by a car or the cavity reaches a deep part, we will also feel pain. The expression of toothache is a warning of impending harm, so that we can find a way to stop it early, so as not to suffer too much damage and be unable to save it in time.

(Question 45) What is the difference between a tooth without pulp and a tooth with intact pulp?

(Answer) The dental pulp is originally a living cell, and the dentin is nourished by it and is also alive. If the dental pulp has a problem and dies, or is extracted! The dentin loses its nourishment and is also dead. At this time, the tooth becomes a dead tooth. Medical treatment to stop tooth pain (39) Li Xing

Amnesia drugs

Scientific advancement is the vanguard of medicine. In the mid-19th century, various scientific developments sprung up like mushrooms after rain. Medical scientists also took the opportunity to use new scientific knowledge to promote and develop medicine, so the inventions in medicine also had the momentum of advancing a thousand miles a day. The most glorious discovery on a page in the history of scientific medicine is the practical application of amnesia drugs. The discovery of amnesia drugs has also opened up a bright road for surgery. Its contribution to mankind is indeed not insignificant. This kind of invention is really worth commemorating, and the process of its discovery is also very interesting.

In 1799, an Englishman named Davy published the amnesic properties of nitrous oxide (i.e., laughing gas) and suggested using nitrous oxide to induce amnesia in patients undergoing surgery. When nitrous oxide is inhaled into the body, the inhaler loses consciousness in an instant, and when he wakes up, he laughs wildly, hence the name laughing gas. Anyone who has studied chemistry a little probably knows this effect of laughing gas. However, scientists are full of research spirit, and Davy wanted to use this gas to induce amnesia in inhalers to eliminate pain. At that time, it was a groundbreaking proposal. Because he was not a doctor, it was not put into practical use. However, this was the prelude to the discovery of amnesia drugs. It was not until 1842 that Dr. Long of Georgia, USA, first used it to induce amnesia in surgical patients.

In December 1844, an American dentist named Wells in Connecticut saw a person lose the sensation of pain after inhaling laughing gas during a lecture and performance. Based on this hint, the next day he used laughing gas to induce amnesia in a patient and then extracted his tooth. After the person woke up, he had no pain at all. This was Wells's great success. Laughing gas then entered the practical application stage. He also immediately wrote books and made great claims about his own talents, forgetting to drink water and think of the source, completely burying the merits of others. Although later commentators did not publicly recognize him as the discoverer of laughing gas, they also recognized his contribution to introducing laughing gas into practical use. Unfortunately, in 1845, the public performance in Boston did not go well and was criticized by the public. At the same time, Morton's performance of inducing amnesia was successful, causing laughing gas to be rejected for many years. Since the failure of his public performance and being ridiculed, Wells became depressed and eventually went mad and committed suicide. Wells's tragic death can also be regarded as a sacrifice for scientific medicine and for the happiness of mankind. This shows that the invention of science is not accidental. Years later, in 1863, Colton (Wells first learned about the use of laughing gas from Colton's performance and used it to highlight his own achievements, burying Colton's merits) revived the use of laughing gas as an amnesia drug and finally achieved success. By 1868, the dental community had widely used laughing gas as an amnesia drug.

A chemist in Boston named Jackson had inhaled an excessive amount of ether in 1841 to lose consciousness, so he suggested using ether as an amnesia drug. He did not put it into practical use himself but introduced this idea to others, one of whom was named Morton. This person and Wells and Jackson were all friends, and he himself was also a dentist. First, Morton learned of Wells's discovery and consulted with Jackson and studied the large-scale production of laughing gas for the world. Jackson suggested manufacturing ether to replace it because it was easy. Later, Morton continued to study ether and finally achieved great success.
