Shen Bao Local Supplement Discussions Let's Save the Students Zi Nan

The other day, Mr. Meng Ruo proposed an idea: abolish the joint entrance examination system, which I think is correct. Joint entrance examinations not only have good points in fact, but also, in order to cope with multiple subjects, one has to take shortcuts, read some joint entrance examination guides or outlines, etc. As a result, the habit of being greedy for the near and easy is developed. The popularity of books like "guides" and "outlines" in the recent publishing industry is the best ironclad proof.

In fact, our education system is not only like this in this one aspect, but also in many other aspects; for example, extracurricular activities are also like this.

Extracurricular activities are probably intended to cultivate good citizens and get used to group life, so there are various organizations of "small governments" and other small groups, forcibly pulling innocent and uncarved children together, as a training for future citizens.

But what is the result? To use a sentence from Meng Ruo, "The disadvantages are so great that the original advocates probably did not expect it."

The original intention of the advocates may be that students cannot find the door to society once they leave the school gate, so they first create a miniature social organization in the school. As a result, a short corridor is named ×× Road, etc., and even a back alley school with only three classrooms actually divides itself into what bureau and what bureau, like a small sparrow with all its internal organs.

This kind of official-style organization, in the end, only cultivates the children's concept of becoming officials, and nothing else can be gained. If you want to say that it is to let them experience social life first, the facts tell you that as long as you step out of the school threshold and step into society, you will open your eyes and see that everything is different, and you will know that the so-called social life in school is not that simple at all.

And in school, since there is such an "organization," what follows is the struggle for power and profit; I remember when I was in school, I personally experienced such a life. At that time, my grade and the highest grade were vying to be the county magistrate. In order to seize the "masses," we went around to mobilize the lower classes, and what we used as bait for mobilization was treating guests, promising to give things to the heads of the lower classes, and contacting athletes as armed bodyguards.

And other than that, all subjects are regarded as secondary.

Therefore, most high school graduates study liberal arts, law, and political economics, because these are close to the "official

path."

"Save the children!" "Save the students!" The Turning Wheel Meng Hua

The wheel kept turning, making a rhythmic creaking sound.

Auntie Li squatted beside the wheel, holding the adobe brick with one hand and carefully grinding and repairing it with a bamboo board with the other. She had been working since morning, and her eyes were already blurred. The wheel under her eyes seemed to be getting bigger and bigger, like a dark cloud, hovering low over this large workshop, making everything around it dark.

The wheel kept turning, and the days were like the turning wheel. Auntie Li's heart was filled with those past events.

"The days spent under the bitter neem tree!" she thought. Her hands had never stopped. When she was a child, when other children were still playing, she would help her mother with work. Many people praised her mother in her face:

"Look at Xiao Tao, she's only ten years old, the time to play, and she can already earn money for her mother!"

"It's the child's bitter fate." Her mother said, sometimes with tears falling down. At that time, the needle in her hand would move even faster. She turned her small hands into mallets. Sometimes she would cry at night, but her mother would feel sorry for her.

Later, her mother died. She also grew up. Her father, who was often angry, always beat her. One day, she was taken away by a stranger.

The wheel was still turning. Auntie Li stood up and used her foot to push it hard. The wheel turned frantically again, creaking.

Auntie Li thought again: Later, people no longer called her Xiao Tao, but called her Auntie Li. Li Si was a good man. He worked in the fields all day long. She also helped him. Her hands had never been idle for a day. Soon, she was the mother of Xiao Shunzi. The three of them lived without happiness or suffering. When Xiao Shunzi was playing, he would pull weeds, scoop water, and pump water in the fields, and also deliver food to his father. People also praised Xiao Shunzi, saying that he could work like an adult at a young age. Although her mother loved her, she still didn't let her steal time to play.

The wheel was still turning, and Auntie Li's eyes felt even more blurred.

She and her man fled the famine. Because it was a famine year, the rice was scorched to death by the sun before it could spike. They begged for food, they worked short-term jobs, helping people with work, and almost sold their children. After another year, when it was almost time to harvest the rice, there was a flood. The water flooded the crops, and the water destroyed her home, drowning the dogs, pigs, and cattle alive. In this way, she and her man fled to a faraway big city. They had no relatives and could not find food to eat. So her man went to work, and she, the girl, worked on the road for people, mending socks, mending shorts, mending gowns, and she was still a twelve-year-old girl. As for herself? She worked as a lady in this porcelain factory, repairing, shaving, and grinding non-stop from morning to night, and it had been almost a year.

"The days spent under the bitter neem tree!" she thought to herself. Her hands had never stopped since she was born.

The wheel kept turning, making a creaking sound. The days were like the turning wheel, passing so quickly.

Auntie Li's eyes were even more blurred. She could hardly see the turning wheel. But her hands were instinctively, subconsciously, grinding and repairing. Her head also ached so much that she felt dizzy and uncomfortable.

The sky was getting dark. The electric lights came on. She stood up and shook herself. "Another day has passed. I don't know if Xiao Shunzi was ridiculed again by others for working today? These days are hard to endure!" Auntie Li thought as she walked out of the factory gate.

The days were like the turning wheel, passing so quickly.

Xiao Shunzi squatted beside the wheel, carefully grinding and repairing the adobe brick with a bamboo board. Her eyes were also blurred. People said that Xiao Shunzi was capable, and she went to work in the factory at the age of thirteen to earn money. But Xiao Shunzi swallowed the tears in her heart and thought, "If I don't work, then I have to eat coal slag!"

When she looked at the wheel, she remembered her mother. "Mom was exhausted to death by these hardships. Now, it's my turn to fill Mom's vacancy. When will the suffering be enough?"

The wheel kept turning, making a rhythmic, creaking sound.

The days were like the turning wheel, passing so quickly.

"Turn! Turn! Turn! Turn as much as you can!" Xiao Shunzi said softly. General Ward Ling Zixi

The lowest-grade ward of the sanatorium, including myself, was tightly packed with eight people. And all eight people had to exhale the breath of their illness in this small room with only two windows. Thinking about it, it was very terrible and very uncomfortable.

We had just finished lunch, and it was still early before the scheduled lunch time. The sky had not been sunny since morning, always with a gloomy look. Moreover, the wind was blowing, and it was raining again. Several patients had not slept well last night, tossing and turning all night. In the morning, they asked the nurse Miss to ask the doctor to come and examine them in a good voice. The doctor came with a displeased look. He scolded several people: "You don't know how to take care of yourselves, and you still cause trouble, always asking for examinations! Haven't you been examined last week? If you want to be examined every day, go live in the first-class ward! You these...!"

The patients closed their mouths like prisoners, and a feeling of fear passed through their bodies, trembling and worrying; God, I hope it's not "you these lowly people"!

"People in the lowest-grade ward are really destined to be lowly people," one person, coughing repeatedly, muttered sadly to himself after the doctor and nurse had left.

No one answered him, and he sighed and slowly began to say: "What a world! In this era, poor people who get rich people's diseases only have death to look forward to. If it weren't for my wife and children being still young, I wouldn't want to come to a sanatorium."

"That's right," an old patient by the window said in a hoarse voice, shaking as he took up his words: "I've been a hard laborer for most of my life, and that's enough. It's not enough to get a body full of diseases. For the sake of my family's livelihood, I have to borrow money to come to a sanatorium, but after three or five months, I still have to go back to hard labor, still have to..."

When a person is over fifty years old, a sense of resentment is added to the sadness.

Hearing these words, several people stared blankly, watching the raindrops pattering on the window.

"Alas," a long sigh floated from the bed in the corner of the room: "Speaking of life, I myself have climbed it like a snail climbing a mountain, steep and strenuous, but I have climbed it for more than thirty years. But who would have thought that I would get this kind of disease from hard labor? People say that this is a rich person's disease. People like us, who are crowded into a small room with seven or eight people, don't get ultraviolet light, don't take expensive tonics, and don't use artificial pneumothorax - inventions that benefit mankind are not for us! Every day we eat a few bowls of porridge, measure our temperature, endure the anger of doctors and nurses, and listen to the groans of others... Do you think there's any use in this? Isn't it just waiting to die? I often think: why bother seeing a doctor when you're living this kind of life?"

"That's right. At this time, it's basically a crime for poor people to get sick! How can we still have the right to be treated?..."

In the corridor, hurried footsteps floated by, and the sounds of talking floated in intermittently: the people in the room were cold at heart, like the wet earth outside, and the rain kept beating down...

The weather was gloomy and cold, and the wind blew in from the window. People shivered with cold. It was already the full mood of early winter. We, a group of people with sick bodies and minds, were thinking about this sick world. It seemed that everything was as bad as we were, and we needed a thorough X-ray examination and enthusiastic ultraviolet light therapy.

There was a soft sound of footsteps outside the door, and the nurse opened the door again, looked around, and then said in a commanding tone: "Quiet! Don't talk too much. How can the patients be allowed to talk so much! It's nap time, everyone has to sleep well!" She came over and pulled up the covers for everyone, and then went out again, slamming the door shut - leaving us inside the door, all silent and quiet.

I fell asleep deeply, but the annoying, cold drizzle was still falling outside. Desolate Village Xiao Qi

The warm sunlight is always so softly illuminating the earth, the trees in the fields are always swaying in various poses in the gentle morning breeze, infused with freshness, and unknown birds are still singing sweetly in the shade of the trees. However, the dynamics of some active people under the sunlight are gradually declining.

Farmers should be like animals all year round, but everyone is willing to be busy with their hands and feet without stopping for a moment, plowing the fields and sowing, scooping water, and cutting seedlings. In those fields and in those seeds, they know that they will be irrigated by their own sweat and strength to produce ears of large millet, which will then turn into shiny gold. They always look forward to this time with pleasant hearts. So the work becomes more and more intense, and the days pass quite energetically. No one has room to worry about anything, but what about now? Everyone is idle and panicked. The thick arms have nowhere to use, so they are only used to beat women when they get angry. Many fields have been abandoned, and grass plants have made their homes. All those who can leave have left, and those who cannot move can only endure the desolate days while half-starving.

The previous beautiful scene is already a dream world.

In the fields, there is no path that has been walked out of the grass, because no one has passed by for a long time, and it is covered by fluffy wild grass. It is still impossible to find the path. Nor are there any shadows of groups of shepherds, riding on the backs of cows, walking while opening their high-pitched voices to sing along with the birds in the shade of the trees. Bare-armed farmers with hoes can only see sparse shadows of a few people in the vast fields. In the past, there would be three or five people in every small field, some pushing shovels to turn the soil, some soaking their legs in the water, pulling weeds, working diligently, with healthy smiles on their faces and murmuring on their lips.

Beside the shallow pond, there are also the lively and cheerful voices of women washing clothes, and the childish and loud laughter.

Where have those healthy smiles and cheerful voices disappeared to? Early in the morning, there is no bustling crowd in the desolate fields, no groups of shepherds, only small birds singing desolately. And from the fields to the village, similarly, on the street, you can no longer see crowded people carrying burdens, especially in the morning, only a few idle people walking around in the cold and quiet. In the endless houses next to each other, although smoke rises from the roofs, you can only see a wisp of black smoke flying away in the fog every ten houses. In front of each house, no one comes out for a long time. Some are even locked, and the door knockers have grown rust. The people here seem to be dwindling day by day, and it seems impossible to make them nostalgic. They are scattering in all directions to other places. From the fields to the city, the villages are gradually deserted. Broadcasting

Song Introduction

The Swallow Tower

The setting sun is late at Wuyi Port, and the wild grass is cold by the Vermilion Bird Bridge. The passing water flows in vain, and the fallen flowers are ruthlessly destroyed. Seeing things and thinking of people makes my heart gloomy, and I can't help but shed red tears on my silk dress. As the saying goes, ill-fated beauties are used to it, but I am not a beauty and my fate is also difficult. The former prosperity turned into fleeting clouds in the blink of an eye, and the long nights are filled with dreams. My shadow is alone, leaving behind loneliness. I only see the swallows returning as before, but they never return. Zhang Shangshu is too wronged, with thousands of sorrows. Twenty years of shared dreams, how can I bear to look back? In the past, I used to get drunk with you, sir, in this tower, knocking on the zither and singing. In the boudoir, behind the beaded curtain, the singing and dancing spread out. It is truly like all the immortals singing the Rainbow Skirt Dance together. I am willing to be like pine and cypress, hoping to be with my pillow and quilt forever, enjoying music and resigning from officialdom, better than being a governor guarding the frontier. Although the spring breeze is blooming with peach and plum blossoms, I also see the autumn rain falling on the leaves of the plane trees. Human fame and fortune are as precious as bubbles, and since ancient times, separation and reunion have been the law of circulation. Even if I meet a kindred spirit, how can I bear to live alone in an empty room? I used to sail in the same boat, and I often sighed to myself. The night is long, the lamp is dim, the more I think, the more I think, again and again. Your kindness is as high as a mountain, and your grace is as deep as the sea. I must repay you. I cannot repay you for wearing a ring and knotting grass. I originally wanted to follow you to the grave, but I am afraid of tarnishing your public image. I am ashamed to steal a life, and it is difficult for me to be a person! Now, I can hardly eat the delicious food, and I am too lazy to play the jade flute and the zither. The embroidered headband, the ruyi hairpin, and the osmanthus comb are still too lazy to dress up. The wedding bed is quickly cleaned up, and it is difficult to sleep in the warm lotus fragrance. From now on, in this Swallow Tower, let the spider webs bury the tracks. I will cut off all ties with the world, and I will have no regrets. I will be a Vermilion Bird flying high, not a fallen phoenix. Special Programs The Nightingale Art Society

Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee to Discuss Next National Games Tomorrow 129

(Nanjing, 3rd) The Ministry of Education's Physical Education Committee is scheduled to hold a committee meeting on the 5th in the Ministry of Education's conference room. A detailed report on the current National Games will be given, and improvements for the next National Games will be discussed.

Chinese Football Matches Not Held Yesterday 130

The Chinese Football Association opened last week. Apart from the two matches between Guanghua Youth and Public Federation Jianmin, all ten matches scheduled for yesterday were cancelled due to overnight rain, which made the fields unsuitable for play. The results of the two matches on the 2nd are listed below: Guanghua defeated Qingguang Middle School Group 7-2; Jianmin defeated Public Federation Society Group 1-0.

Zhejiang Province Stadium Creates Mechanical Exercise Area 131

(Hangzhou News) The Zhejiang Provincial Stadium, in order to promote public exercise, has built a public mechanical exercise area at the end of the stadium's baseball field. Construction began two months ago and is expected to be completed within this month, with a formal opening scheduled. At that time, residents of Hangzhou and students from various elementary schools will be invited to participate in activities to promote the initiative.

Guanghua, Shanghai College, Middle School and Others to Have New Sports Organization - Nanyang Model and Fudan Affiliated High Schools in Talks, Emphasizing Spiritual Organization Similar to China Sports Federation - Guanghua and Shanghai College Basketball Friendly Match Tomorrow 132

Guanghua University on Daxilu has seen its sports program flourish since the establishment of its new gymnasium, emphasizing universality by hosting various open ball games, with over thirty participating teams. An average of three open games are held each day. According to Mr. Jiang Jingnan, coach of Guanghua, to the Guoguang News Agency, the school is planning to jointly launch a sports association with Provincial Shanghai College, Shanghai College Affiliated Middle School, Nanyang Model Middle School, or Fudan Affiliated Middle School, similar to the China Sports Federation, focusing on the spirit of practical sports rather than championships. Provincial Shanghai College and Shanghai College have already reached maturity and will join. Nanyang Model and Fudan Affiliated Middle Schools are still in discussions. Regulations will soon be drafted and announced. Tomorrow (Tuesday) at 3:00 PM, Guanghua is scheduled to play a friendly basketball game with Shanghai College at the Guanghua Gymnasium, which is said to be a precursor to the new organization.

Hard Court Tennis Postponed Due to Rain 134

Yesterday, the hard court tennis semi-finals, which were originally scheduled to be held at the French Chamber of Commerce, with sixteen matches of men's and women's singles and doubles, starting at 10:00 AM, had to be temporarily postponed due to rain and wet fields. According to the person in charge of the French Chamber of Commerce, if the weather clears up within a few days, the games can be made up immediately; otherwise, they will be postponed until next Saturday.

Youyou and Jinan University Football Teams Go to Suzhou to Participate in Disaster Relief Competition 135

The Youyou and Jinan University football teams went to Suzhou to participate in a disaster relief competition, which caused a sensation in the city. Mr. Wu Silan, a Suzhou gentleman, has agreed to personally donate all travel and meal expenses for both teams. All ticket revenue will be used for disaster relief. All procedures have been prepared. It is also planned that Mr. Wu Silan will host a banquet for the team members at the Liu Garden after they get off the bus. After the competition, Mr. Wu Silan will host a dinner party at his private residence.

The Malaysian-Chinese Athletes Delegation Returns South on the 8th 136

The Malaysian-Chinese athletes delegation attending this National Games went to Beijing for sightseeing after the closing ceremony. They have now returned to Shanghai a few days ago and are still residing at the Liangjiang Sports School. It has been decided that they will return south on the Italian mail ship Conte Rosso on the 8th. It is reported that the team has been extremely busy with banquets and competitions in recent days and now plans to rest in Shanghai for a few days without making any more competitions or visits. In addition, Mr. Diao Zuqian, Consul-General of Singapore, is also scheduled to leave Shanghai and return to Singapore with the athletes delegation on the 8th.
